Siam Used by Japan 36

Kra Isthmus Canal to be Built

Connecting the Indian Ocean and the China Sea

Japan Plans to Establish Secret Naval Base

(London) The government of Siam has decided to build a canal across the Kra Isthmus (this isthmus is located between Burma and the Malay Peninsula) to connect the Indian Ocean and the China Sea. According to a report in the Conservative Party's newspaper, the Daily Express, this canal is no less than the "Kiel Canal of Asia" (the Kiel Canal is located in northern Germany and connects the North Sea and the Baltic Sea). The funds are provided by Japan. This move is intended by the Japanese to counter Britain, as Britain recently decided to complete the Singapore naval base as soon as possible. The newspaper believes that Japan intends to use Siam for foreign expansion, regarding it as a base in the South Seas, etc. (Havas dispatch on the 22nd)

(London) A traveling reporter for the London Daily Express telegraphed from Singapore that the Japanese are now actively seeking a suitable location for a secret naval base. The Japanese are currently negotiating to build a canal through the Kra Neck in southern Burma, so that ships docked at the secret base can avoid the Strait of Malacca between Malaysia and Sumatra. At the same time, according to a Reuters dispatch from Brisbane, Australia, the Australian ship Mildred reported that a Japanese ship was engaged in secret work. Its crew of about 30 people was seen near Cairns on the coast of Queensland, seemingly collecting shellfish, but they did not allow anyone to approach, otherwise they would open fire. The Japanese are all carrying rifles and pistols. (Reuters dispatch on the 22nd)

Japan to Increase Troops in Northeast 37

Committee to Study Military System Reform

Army Ministry Undertakes Large-Scale Military Reorganization

(Tokyo) After the Manchurian Incident, the Army authorities temporarily implemented the strengthening of troops stationed in Manchuria, reformed various systems, and prepared materials using funds for the current situation and military preparations. However, now that the incident has been resolved, it is planned to change the temporary measures into a permanent system. The Army Ministry, the General Staff Headquarters, the Inspectorate General of Military Education, and other top army organs are scheduled to establish a committee after the end of the Diet to study the military system reform plan. The main items to be reviewed by the committee are the "Manchukuo" national defense joint defense issue stipulated in the Japan-Manchukuo Protocol, the standing army force to deal with internal and external situations, the garrison force in "Manchukuo," and other matters. It is reported that because Japan bears the important task of jointly defending "Manchukuo," it is necessary to permanently station several divisions in "Manchukuo." Therefore, the increase of the standing army force is a necessary matter to be implemented. (Japan United Press dispatch on the 22nd)

(Tokyo) Regarding the use of 120 million yen for military equipment preparation in the Army Ministry's next year's budget, after research, it has been decided to allocate the quantity to be made to various private military factories. Forty supervisors will be appointed soon to investigate the technical and accounting aspects of each factory from April 1st. (Japan United Press dispatch on the 22nd)

Anglo-Russian Commercial Treaty Initialed 38

(London) The Anglo-Russian commercial treaty, which was signed on February 16th, was initialed with Moscow today. (Reuters dispatch on the 21st)

Understanding Reached Between US and Japan, Pacific Situation Suddenly Changes 39

Ten-Nation Conference to be Held Next Year

To Handle All Far Eastern Problems

The US Will Not Lightly Show Its Hand Until the Unveiling

US and Japan Make Further Consultations to Improve Relations

(London) A Washington dispatch from the London Morning Post states that there will be no new developments in US-Japan relations until Japanese Ambassador to the US, Saito, returns to Tokyo to consult with the Japanese government. It is becoming increasingly clear that a new Pacific conference will be held at the same time as the Maritime Disarmament Conference next year. In addition to the five powers of Britain, Japan, France, Italy, and the US, China, Belgium, the Netherlands, Portugal, and Russia will also participate. At that time, international problems such as the recognition of "Manchukuo" will be handled. However, the US will not show its hand until after the unveiling. The US remains indifferent to Japan's seizure of the British textile market in the Far East, because if Britain buys less US cotton, Japan will buy more. However, US rubber products and electrical appliances have recently been facing competition from Japanese goods, which the US cannot sit idly by and watch. (Reuters dispatch on the 22nd)

(London) According to reliable sources today, consultations between the US and Japan regarding Pacific security and US-Japan relations, due to the exchanges between US Secretary of State Hull and Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota (according to yesterday's report, what Japan wants is the amendment of the US immigration law, the abandonment of US naval and air bases, and US recognition of "Manchukuo," Japan will exchange this by recognizing the current 5:5:3 naval ratio), Hirota and Hull's preliminary consultations have shown smooth progress, then Japanese Ambassador to the US Saito will prepare to have further discussions directly with Hull to seek to stabilize and improve US-Japan relations. Regarding the US abandonment of naval and air bases in the Philippines, it is widely believed that Japan is willing to guarantee the neutrality of the Philippines and will be prepared to abandon its insistence on naval parity with Britain and the US at the fourth naval conference to be held in 1935, and is willing to maintain the originally stipulated 5:5:3 naval ratio limit. This move is intended to dispel outside fears of a naval race and dispel the clouds of war in the Pacific. If the US-Japan negotiations in the US are successful, then the US and Japan may conclude a non-aggression treaty. (National News Agency dispatch on the 22nd)

(Washington) US newspapers and key figures in Congress have unanimously expressed their appreciation for the report on the consultations between Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota and US Secretary of State Hull, and see this as a ray of hope for the development of the Pacific situation, and the reconciliation of disputes between the US and Japan may be led by this. A spokesman for the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, in an interview with the Associated Press, praised the exchanges between Hull and Hirota, believing that the US will discuss the differences between the two countries with an attitude of candor and sincerity. Republican leader Borah, known for his expertise in diplomacy, also said of the US-Japan consultations that it was like hearing the music of heaven, which was indeed pleasing to the ear, but what kind of impact it would have on the naval arms race was the touchstone of the recent consultations between the two countries. Senator Robinson said that if the consultations led to peace, he would also support them. According to government sources, the initiation of the consultations was by the US and not Japan, especially with regard to proposals to increase and maintain friendship between the two countries. Observers believe that all countries related to the Far East should participate in the US-Japan discussions. It is also said that in the reply, the US stated that the solution to the Pacific problem must be bound by existing treaties, because this is a multilateral issue rather than a purely US-Japan bilateral issue. Although there is much speculation here about the act of recognizing "Manchukuo," it is believed that the US may not take this step without the participation of China and the Soviet Union. (National Telegraph dispatch on the 22nd)

(New York) The New York Public Voice Forum published an editorial stating that the exchange of letters between the US Secretary of State and Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota is sufficient to show that the friendship between the two countries has been placed on a solid foundation, and the doubts held by the Japanese regarding the purpose of the US Far Eastern policy may be dispelled by the publication of these two letters. The newspaper also stated that opinions from well-informed sources in Japan also know that the US naval construction plan, aimed at reaching the treaty limit, does not mean changing the situation in the Pacific. On the contrary, this is merely a precaution. Only in this way can the US stand on an equal footing with Britain and Japan at the upcoming naval conference. (Havas dispatch on the 21st)

(Washington) Secretary of the Navy Swanson declared that he believes that the US and Japan should hold preliminary talks on naval affairs before the Washington Naval Conference of 1935, and that the current ratio of naval forces between Britain, the US, and Japan should be maintained. (Havas dispatch on the 21st)

(Washington) According to Japanese Ambassador to the US Saito, as a result of US-Japan friendship, the US may abandon its policy of rejecting the immigration of Japanese people to the US, which is greatly dissatisfied with by the Japanese people. Saito also said that he was very pleased to learn that the major powers are willing to follow the US's lead and no longer restrict the entry of Japanese people. He said that he does not want to force countries to amend their laws, as this matter is purely in the hands of the national parliaments. Saito also said that if the US can change its attitude, the Japanese people will benefit greatly and will deeply appreciate the kindness and fairness of the American people, and the friendship between the two countries will be greatly enhanced. This approach is not only a desire of Japan, but also an established policy. As for the foreign trade of Britain and the US, it may become an all-out battle in the future. Saito said that this was inaccurate, because Britain and the US are relatively good customers of each other, and the same is true in the Pacific, because the US and Japan are also relatively good customers of each other. Finally, Saito also dismissed rumors of an imminent Russo-Japanese war as unfounded. (National News Agency dispatch on the 22nd)

(Washington) Mrs. President Roosevelt hosted a banquet at the White House today to entertain Japanese Ambassador to the US Saito and his wife. The event was very grand and lively. (National Telegraph dispatch on the 21st)

Gleanings from British Newspapers 41

(London) The natural result of the exchange of letters between US Secretary of State Hull and Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota will be the US's recognition of "Manchukuo." All British newspapers, regardless of their party affiliation, answer this question in the affirmative. The Morning Post, which has always been known for its strong advocacy of British-Japanese friendship, even takes the actions on the other side of the Atlantic as a model and earnestly urges the British cabinet to give it deep consideration. The Conservative Party newspaper said that the Washington government's recognition of the puppet empire in the near future is inevitable. Former Secretary of State Stimson's doctrine of non-recognition is like an idol that has been destroyed, and President Roosevelt is the first to worship this idol. Therefore, Britain has no choice but to wander alone by the shores of Lake Leman, holding on to the remnants of the so-called non-recognition doctrine, adhering to its service unswervingly. The US, which had previously exhausted its efforts to isolate Japan, has now changed its attitude and abandoned this dangerous political error. Therefore, the Japanese, who held an unfair feeling that the US policy was like throwing poison and leaving a great disaster in the Pacific, have been comforted. This is undoubtedly gratifying. Another Conservative Party newspaper, the Daily Telegraph, although not taking such a stance, also believes that if the US can obtain guarantees for the open door and economic concessions in the eastern provinces, it may abandon its policy of non-recognition in exchange. However, it believes that the White House will not rashly follow this path without first seeking the opinion of the League of Nations "Committee on Non-Recognition of Manchukuo." The Liberal Party newspaper, the News Chronicle, while firmly believing that the Washington government will work hard to get the Chinese government to recognize it on its own, also believes that Japan may abandon its demands on naval tonnage ratios at the 1935 Disarmament Conference as an exchange condition. (Havas dispatch on the 22nd)

US Big Navy Bill 42

Republican Congressmen Criticize as Merely Increasing the Burden

Amendment Returned to the Senate

(Washington) The House today rejected the Senate's amendment to the $500 million naval expansion bill and returned the bill to the Senate for further discussion of differences. The bill stipulates a large-scale program for building warships and aircraft. It was passed by the Senate with some amendments on March 6. The amendments include: (1) profits obtained by private contractors may not exceed 10 percent, (2) the government should only manufacture one-quarter of the 1,000 aircraft originally stipulated in the plan. Republican Senator Nye has criticized the bill as a grandiose statement and a bill aimed at rescuing workers manufacturing weapons, saying that the bill will increase the nation's burden by $100 million, as the bill stipulates the construction of six cruisers, thirty submarines, sixty-five destroyers, and one aircraft carrier over five years. (Reuters dispatch on the 21st)

British Prime Minister's Speech Defending Increased Defense Spending 43

Naval Program Does Not Exceed Treaty Limits

Expressing Willingness to Strive to Maintain the Authority of the League of Nations

(London) Today, British Prime Minister MacDonald delivered cautionary remarks in the House of Commons, defending the increase in naval, land, and air force expenditures, saying that Britain's current consideration of armaments is not intended to harm other countries, but to meet its own national defense needs. Britain's desire to limit armaments by treaty is for this reason. Now, in order to reduce danger, it is necessary to do so, but Britain still trusts treaties. Britain's naval program strictly does not exceed the scope of the naval treaty. However, the government must increase its tools to protect civilians and defend against aerial attacks. This kind of danger may not materialize for the time being, but it cannot be ignored, because even a slight negligence will have terrible consequences. Britain's only aim is peace based on international cooperation and the League of Nations. If the League of Nations is used well, it is the only mechanism to achieve this goal. Therefore, the British government will strive to maintain the authority of the League of Nations. Lord President of the Council Baldwin, speaking to conclude the defense debate, said that the method of international management of civil aviation to eliminate the harm of aerial attacks is impossible. He had suggested this method two years ago to seek a solution. The government immediately studied the matter and planned measures. Drafts were repeatedly changed, taking a lot of time, but after painstaking efforts, it still felt that it could not get a satisfactory solution, and no other country had put forward any plan that could be implemented or could solve this problem. (Reuter, 21st)

Unprecedented Fire in Hakodate City, Japan 46

Blown-Down Chimney Instantly Becomes a Prairie Fire

Wind Assists the Fire's Power, Burning Day and Night

23,000 Households in the Entire City Reduced to Ashes

More Than a Thousand Dead and Injured, Material Losses of 100 Million

Aomori At 6:50 pm on the 21st, a chimney in a bathhouse in Sumiyoshi Town, Hakodate City, suddenly caught fire. At that time, a strong wind of 30 meters was already raging, and in an instant, it spread to the entire city. More than 60 towns including Aoyagi, Akebono, Bunken, Aioi, and Kotobuki Town were all reduced to ashes. The cries of women were unbearable to hear. Due to the disruption of communication organs, the details are unknown. At 4:30 am on the 22nd, it was still burning. According to a report from the Sapporo Railway Bureau received by the Ministry of Railways, there were more than 1,000 deaths and injuries, and approximately 24,500 households were burned. (Dentsu, 22nd)

Tsuruga According to Wakasa Radio, a telegram was received at 6:40 am this morning stating that Hakodate City has been 80% destroyed. The wind is gradually weakening, there are 150,000 victims, and there are many deaths and injuries, which are difficult to count. Another telegram stated that the Hakodate fire was extinguished at 7:00 am this morning. (Nichi-Ren, 22nd)

(Tokyo) At 7:12 pm today, the Ministry of Home Affairs announced the following damages from the Hakodate fire: 23,600 households destroyed, a disaster-stricken population of 92,000, 650 deaths, 460 injuries, and 32 shelters with a total of 27,000 people. (Dentsu, 22nd)

(Tokyo) According to a message sent by the Sapporo Broadcasting Station at 8:10 pm this afternoon, more than 140,000 Hakodate refugees are being housed in 32 places such as elementary schools, and are only given three meals a day. The refugees are suffering from hunger and cold, and women and children are especially pitiful. According to news received by the Wakasa Radio Telegraph Office, the losses suffered in this fire alone have reached 30 million yen for various insurance companies. If each household is counted at 500 yen, it exceeds 100 million yen. The army, navy, Ministry of Home Affairs, and Ministry of Railways have all increased their rescue teams. It is reported that the consulates and commercial agencies of Britain, Russia, and China are safe and sound. (Hua-Lian, 22nd)

(Tokyo) According to the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, the damage from the Hakodate city fire is estimated to be no less than 20 million yen. Japanese fire insurance companies all consider Hakodate to be the most dangerous place. Assuming that the insurance premiums for this fire are 10 million yen, it accounts for half of the average annual expenditure of 20 million yen for national insurance companies. The largest record of insurance payments in Japan, apart from the Kanto earthquake, was 6 million yen during the Osaka fire 18 years ago. During the fire at the Shirokiya department store in Tokyo the year before last, the Daito and Nissho companies paid 2.3 million yen in insurance, leading to bankruptcy. After the news of the Hakodate fire was released, various insurance companies were panicked. (Nichi-Ren, 22nd)

(Tokyo) The Japanese Ministry of the Navy received a telegram for help from the governor of Hokkaido last night. Navy Minister Osumi immediately mobilized the First Destroyer Division to dispatch. It is reported that four Japanese warships, including the Kamikaze, were ordered to sail to Hakodate this morning. The army also sent Type 88 reconnaissance aircraft to fly over Hakodate to investigate the disaster situation and report to various agencies to facilitate relief. According to a report from the Tsugaru Fortress Command, the important organs of the Hakodate Army have not been burned as of this morning, but the army officers' dormitory has been completely destroyed. (Hua-Lian, 22nd)

(Tokyo) According to a telegram from Wakasa Wireless Radio Station on the outskirts of Hakodate City to Tokyo, the Hakodate fire, fanned by strong winds, continued until 5:30 am today, burning two-thirds of the city's 40,000 households before it was extinguished. Only Benten Town and Suehiro Town have not been completely burned. The entire city is now a vast expanse. Even the famous Goryokaku has been burned. As of 4:00 am today, approximately 24,500 households have been burned, more than 1,000 people have been killed or injured, and 150,000 victims have been left homeless, standing in the wilderness, suffering from hunger and cold. The scene is too terrible to describe. Important buildings that have been burned include the city hall, such as the Jitsugyo High School, Girls' High School, Nishihonganji Betsuin Temple, Broadcasting Station, Postal Bureau, Elementary School, Hakodate Shimbun, Hakodate Mainichi Shimbun, various government offices, etc. However, the consulates of various countries are located on the hillside and have been spared. The cause of the fire was that the chimney of the Sumiyoshi Town bathhouse was blown down by the wind, causing the fire. At that time, the southeast wind in Hakodate was strong, and the wind speed was still 30 meters at 5:00 am. The fire from the chimney was fanned by the wind and spread very quickly in an instant. In addition, the submarine cable also experienced an obstacle due to the strong wind at 11:00 pm last night, and communication was impossible, completely cutting off direct contact with Aomori City. Originally, Hakodate City was famous for fires, and burning 500 or 600 households was not considered a major fire, but the most recent record was 2,140 households burned on April 14, 1922, with losses of 18.5 million yen. However, compared to this fire, it pales in comparison. The total fire insurance amount in Hakodate City reaches more than 30 million yen, so insurance companies are panicking. Also, the Hakodate Fortress Command and the barracks of the heavy artillery unit seem to be safe. (Dentsu, 22nd)

Hakodate The Hakodate fire spread very quickly due to the strong wind and fierce fire. The victims had no time to take out all their property from their homes and flocked to Omori Beach for refuge, just like the clothing factory during the Tokyo earthquake. Omori Beach was also burned, and those who fled had nowhere to go. Some were burned to death, and some drowned in the sea. It was like Avici hell, and it was unbearable to witness. Therefore, there were many deaths in that area. In addition, all the prisoners in the Hakodate Prison were also released. The scope of the fire was three cho (more than 1,000 feet) wide and one and a half ri long. The losses are difficult to estimate. (Dentsu, 22nd)

(Tokyo) To rescue the Hakodate fire disaster, at 2:35 pm today, the Ministry of Railways specially opened a rescue train from Ueno Station in the city. Director Haneda of the Social Bureau of the Ministry of Home Affairs and other officials, nurses, and other rescue teams, as well as 720 news reporters, departed on this train and rushed to Aomori City, and then took a boat from Aomori to Hakodate to rescue the victims, scheduled to arrive in Hakodate City tomorrow afternoon. (Hua-Lian, 22nd)

(Tokyo) According to a report from the Hokkaido Prefectural Office to the Ministry of Home Affairs, the Hakodate fire is beyond salvage. The victims are extremely exhausted in the wind and rain. The government first purchased 6,000 bags of rice and mobilized youth groups and rural soldiers to cook outdoors to provide emergency relief. Martial law was declared throughout the city, and troops and police officers were ordered to maintain order and provide relief to the victims. They also sought help from the army and navy to cooperate in fighting the fire and disaster relief. The Ministry of Railways also compiled an emergency train to evacuate the refugees, and the entire city has become a field of rubble. (Hua-Lian, 22nd)

(Tokyo) The entire city of Hakodate was swallowed by flames. The authorities released the local prison this morning. The prisoners went out and acted recklessly. Having suffered a major disaster and being disturbed by prisoners, people were very panicked, presenting an increasingly chaotic and volatile scene. The Hakodate Heavy Artillery Brigade, seeing the seriousness of the situation, has also been fully mobilized to assist the police in enforcing martial law, but it is not enough to cope. The 5th Infantry Regiment of Aomori sent 60 people this afternoon, and the 8th Division of Hirosaki sent 100 people to the city. The Asahikawa Division is also preparing to send troops to assist. (Hua-Lian, 22nd)

Hurricane Disaster in Japan 47

(Tokyo) Since the morning of the 21st, Japan has been attacked by strong winds across the country, with a wind speed of 20 meters. The damage has spread throughout the country. The Kan-Fu connection route, the Inland Sea-Kyushu route, the Kanmon connection ship, and others have all been suspended. In the Ishikawa Prefecture area, more than 500 houses in Daishoji Town were flooded, embankments collapsed, and bridges were washed away. In Taiwan, three fishing boats were overturned off the coast of Keelung, eight people were rescued, and seven people were missing. Near Tokyo, at the Yaguchi Ferry on the Tama River, all 120 gravel boats were also suspended. In the Ibaraki Prefecture area, the school building of the Yunosawa Village Elementary School in Makabe County and the newly built school building of the Taniida Village Elementary School in Tsukuba County were both blown down. The number of telegram and telephone damage accidents is even innumerable. The triumphal arch in Hirosaki City was destroyed. The wind speed in Aomori City was 25 meters, and in addition, snow was melting, and many houses were flooded. (Dentsu, 22nd)

Roosevelt Tries to Curb the Strike Wave 49

The rumored strikes in the automotive and railway industries are even more serious. The strike situation of 200,000 textile workers in the western United States is also continuing to increase. The workers in the steel industry are also unstable, and the blood-wolf gate strike on the west coast is also on the verge of breaking out. Also, the president has no intention of promoting the approach between labor and management under the current situation. The president's actions must be taken after understanding what concessions both labor and management will make. Today, the American Federation of Labor stated that it could temporarily postpone the request for workers to elect representatives to negotiate with employers as a group and organize workers' grievance groups. The Railway Workers Union has accepted the mediation proposal of Federal Transport Facilitator Esben to resolve the railway industry wage dispute, which is a good sign in the railway industry strike brewing. However, under the current situation, the union side is generally unwilling to have any negotiations with representatives of the railway authorities. Today, Gormen, vice chairman of the Textile Workers Union, told the Senate Workers Committee that 200,000 textile workers are angry and preparing to strike because employers have jointly refused to recognize their union. Senator General Bora attacked the combination of industrialists and condemned them for being greedy and responsible for the entire labor unrest. Prague Rumors of a Secret Military Pact Signed by Italy, Austria, and Hungary 52

Prague There are rumors in the Czech capital that during the Rome Conference, the prime ministers of Italy, Austria, and Hungary signed a military agreement in addition to various treaties. Benes's One-Night Talk Causes Surprise in Hungary 53

Except for the Economic Cooperation Little Agreement

Czech Foreign Minister Believes it is a Source of Disaster

Budapest Czech Foreign Minister Benes gave a speech on the Austrian issue to the Foreign Affairs Committee of the House of Representatives yesterday, saying that there are four solutions to the Austrian issue, and that the Czech government is prepared to participate in various discussions so as to reopen commercial negotiations with Hungary in the near future. Recently, the Czech government made a formal request to Hungary to start negotiations, first to establish a temporary agreement, and then to conclude a commercial treaty. The political and economic circles here were quite surprised to hear this. (Havas, 22nd)

Prague Czech Foreign Minister Benes gave his long-awaited speech today at the Foreign Affairs Committee of the two Houses of Congress. Mr. Benes expressed deep concern about the future war in Europe, and still adhered to his firm attitude towards the consistency of the current situation in Europe. Therefore, he opposed the revision of the peace treaty on the one hand, and repeatedly stated his difficulty in turning a blind eye to the merger of Germany and Austria on the other. Mr. Benes first discussed the previously proposed German-Austrian customs union. He said that the combination had created economic, political and psychological errors. However, the merger of Germany and Austria today is more dangerous than before, and the idea of ​​his suggestion is also different from before, because its purpose is to spread its national social movement widely within Europe, so that a kind of refined association can be achieved between the two countries in order to achieve the final political integration.

This kind of change, in the eyes of Mr. Benes, will inevitably cause a major conflict in the European political situation, but fortunately, he knows that Italy, France, Britain and other related countries will never make the slightest concession to the necessity of maintaining Austria's independence and integrity. Even if Austria temporarily becomes a national socialist country, it will not change its position. Mr. Benes then extended his condolences to Germany, saying that although Germany cannot implement its policy of merger, there is still considerable compensation, that is, Austria must not merge with any political and economic organization to oppose Germany. The current Austrian problem can only be solved by the joint agreement of Rome, Paris, Berlin and the Little Entente countries. However, if the current chaotic situation continues to exist, it will inevitably cause major disputes in the future, because the previous war was caused in Serbia, and the future war may originate in Austria. Mr. Benes did not say that the various principles and obligations of the Geneva Treaty of 1922 concerning the Austrian issue should be fully recognized by all relevant countries, and should not be limited to the four signatory countries. As for the recent Rome Three-Power Conference, Mr. Benes adopted a cautious attitude. He said that the Little Entente countries may not fully agree with Italy's enthusiasm for solving the Danube River basin problem, but his final judgment must wait for the Rome agreement to be specified in the future, and its legal, political and economic effects will be obvious before it can be decided. Furthermore, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini once stated that the establishment of the Rome Agreement did not conflict with the interests of the Little Entente countries. Mr. Benes expressed his welcome to this, but unfortunately, the possibility of the Little Entente countries being added has been reduced by Mussolini's subsequent declaration (Guomin Dian, 22nd).

Japanese Troops Advance in Eastern Chahar 90

Li Shouxin Assumes Position as Commander of the Puppet Chahar Garrison

Japanese Army Personnel, Yuan Ye, Organize Investigation Group to Enter Mongolia

Beiping Correspondence: Japanese troops in eastern Chahar claim that the 8th Division and 7th Division are exchanging deployments in Guyuan and Duolun. However, the 7th Division has successively arrived in the Duozhan area, numbering nearly 1,000 men, while there has been no news of the departure of the 8th Division units originally stationed there. According to recent reports, the headquarters of the Japanese 10th Division has decided to establish itself in Duolun, and the entire division will be stationed in the Duo-Gu area. In addition, there are more than 9,000 men of the puppet army under Li Shouxin, who has assumed the position of Commander of the Puppet Eastern Chahar Garrison. Duolun is an important town in eastern Chahar and a transportation hub between Rehe and Chahar. The Japanese side's gathering of a large army to station in that area certainly has major intentions. The plan is roughly centered on Duolun, developing southward from the second and fourth districts of Guyuan (i.e., the seat of Xinyuan County), and northward from Duolun through the Su-Zhi-Pang-Jiang area of the Xilin Gol League, directly threatening Ude in the Chechen Khanate of Outer Mongolia. Ude is a transportation hub between Inner and Outer Mongolia and is especially a necessary route to Kulun. The arrival of the Japanese army there can cut off Sino-Russian transportation and threaten the Soviet Union. Song Zheyuan, Chairman of Chahar Province, especially accompanied Xiao Zhenying of the Military Commission to the Ju Ren Tang to meet with He Yingqin at 9:00 AM yesterday to report on the issue of the increased Japanese troops in eastern Chahar and requested instructions on how to deal with it. He stated that he had asked the Political Readjustment Council to be responsible for negotiating with the Japanese side to withdraw the troops. Furthermore, Qin Dechun, in response to Song's telegram, arrived in Beiping from Zhangjiakou by fast train at 9:30 AM yesterday. At noon yesterday, he accompanied Song and Huang Fu to a banquet and discussed diplomatic issues in Chahar Province. Song, Qin, and Xiao will stay in Beiping for a few days, and will return to Zhangjiakou after the defense of eastern Chahar has been arranged.

According to news from important Mongolian figures, the Japanese army's invasion of Chahar is aimed at Western Mongolia. On the 7th of this month, Japanese Lieutenant General Yuan Ye organized a so-called "Mongolia Investigation Group" in Changchun. A total of twelve people participated, including one descendant of the Qing Dynasty, two Japanese army strategists, three Japanese geographers, and three Mongolian staff members. They traveled from Changchun through Taonan and Rehe to the Xilin Gol League and Ulanqab League. It is estimated that they have now arrived in eastern Chahar. (March 21st)

Inquired in Detail about the Defenses of Various Units

At 4:30 AM on the 16th, Chiang Kai-shek received Huang Jie, commander of the 2nd Division of Hebei, Liu Duoquan, commander of the 105th Division, Liu Hedong, commander of the 107th Division, Yang Zhengzhi, commander of the 108th Division, Dong Yingbin, commander of the 111th Division, Zhou Fucheng, commander of the 129th Division, Huang Guanghua, commander of the 139th Division, Zhang Binde, commander of the 1st Cavalry Division, Guo Xidiao, commander of the 4th Cavalry Division, Liang Kai, commander of the 67th Brigade of the 25th Division, and Qiao Fang, Zhu Hongxun, and others in his residence, and inquired in detail about the defensive areas, military training, and living conditions of the soldiers of the above generals. Currently, the generals of Hebei, such as Liu Duoquan, have already returned to their defenses, and the rest will also return to their defenses successively. The second and third batches will also come to Jiangxi in a few days. (March 18th)

Yang Jie's Letter Reporting on Italian Military Affairs 92

Highly Praising the Completeness of Italian Military Affairs

And Deeply Admiring Mussolini as a Person

Yang Jie, President of the Army University, has been inspecting military affairs in various European and American countries for nearly three months. Yesterday, Zhang Qiazhong, Director of Education at the Central Military Academy, received a letter from Yang from Berlin, describing in detail his observations of the Army, Navy, Air Force, Party Army, engineering projects, aviation industry, automobile industry, shipbuilding industry, etc. in Rome and other places. The original letter is transcribed below:

My respects to Mr. Wenbai,

It has been two months since we parted in the capital. I miss our old friendship deeply. I arrived in Rome at 9:00 AM on December 9th of last year. Before unpacking, I was guided by Liu Wendao, the Minister to Italy, and representatives from the Italian military to begin the inspection according to Mussolini's scheduled itinerary. The first place shown to me was the world-renowned Air Force Department. Afterwards, I met with Mussolini, the intention being to give me the deepest impression. From the 9th to the 11th, I was in Rome. On the 12th, I was in Terni. On the 13th, I was in Livorno. On the 14th, I was in La Spezia. On the 15th, I was in Genoa. On the 16th, I was in Turin. On the 18th and 19th, I was in Milan and Brescia. I spent a total of eleven days in Italy, studying all aspects of the Army, Navy, Air Force, Party Army, and military industries. I obtained a wealth of material. I left Italy at 12:00 PM on the 19th, stayed in Geneva for a day to visit the League of Nations, and arrived in Berlin on the 22nd. On January 8th of this year, I continued my work. Except for the observations at the League of Nations, which were irrelevant to military affairs, and the inspection of Germany, which is not yet completed, I will briefly present my observations in Italy below:

The Italian military is centered on the royal family and based on the Fascist Party. The relationship between superiors and subordinates is one of solemnity and kindness, while subordinates show respect and love for their superiors. The superiors have a way to command, and the subordinates understand the meaning of obedience. The spirit is vigorous, and the actions are swift. The Army, Navy, and Air Force are divided into three parts. The Army is divided into thirteen military districts and thirty division districts. Officer training is carried out in specialized military universities and schools, with the Minister responsible for everything.

The Navy is divided into four coastal defense sectors, each with a commander-in-chief responsible for their respective areas. Talent is cultivated by the Naval Academy, the Naval Junior School, the Naval Senior Class, and Naval University students, directly under the Minister of the Navy.

The Air Force is divided into three air territory zones and three auxiliary zones. Part of its forces belong to the Army, Navy, and colonies, but the majority is directly under the Air Force Department. The establishment of talent and all organizational construction are under the full responsibility of the Minister of the Air Force. Regarding education, there are Air Force Universities for fighter, reconnaissance, bombing, air force weaponry, air force mechanics, and military training teams, etc.

The Party Army is a special organization, subordinate to the Party, responsible for training young people within the Party. There is a Party Army organization in every city, town, and village in the country. Important cities also have Party Army camps. The scale and equipment are no different from those of the regular army. The current commander-in-chief of the Party Army is an army lieutenant colonel. It is said that if there is a personnel change one day, he will return to his original position as a lieutenant colonel to perform his duties.

The armaments industry also has its merits. Its aviation industry is thriving. The most unique aspect nationwide is that it has achieved self-sufficiency. Aircraft manufacturers include Caproni, Fiat-Breda, and other factories. Among them, Caproni's reputation is particularly well-known domestically. However, due to a lack of light metal resources, they are forced to continue using wood. However, wood is far cheaper than metal, and its use is also a way to solve difficulties. All types of aircraft manufactured by each factory must first be sent to the National Aircraft Testing Ground to check their performance before they are allowed to be replicated or used. As for the new models built by the Air Force Department, the completeness of pneumatic and electrical equipment is unparalleled in the world, and the large number of aircraft is also impressive. The automobile industry is also booming throughout Italy. Fiat alone produces an average of 150 vehicles per day during peacetime and up to 350 vehicles during wartime. Its eight-wheeled large vehicles can accommodate as many as eighty passengers on just one level. In addition, snow transport vehicles, mountain climbing vehicles, tractors, and tanks are also quite developed, but they cannot be compared with the aviation industry. As for the shipbuilding industry, Italy's territory is mostly coastal, so its importance is natural. However, the recent trend is not to focus on maximum tonnage but on maximum speed. The improvement of ship shapes is being studied in great depth. Various types of ships are navigated in the water tank of the testing ground, and the resistance of water is measured mechanically to find the ship type with the least resistance. According to experts, the results obtained after the ship shape improvement are better than simply increasing horsepower, and the speed is even higher in certain situations. In addition, the construction of docks, shipyards, and wharves seeks to be both high-quality and low-cost. The two wharves in La Spezia are solid in content and beautiful in appearance, unmatched in the modern world. This is also a successful construction since Mussolini came to power. Regarding the manufacture of guns, cannons, bullets, etc., since the Great War, the working capacity has been reduced by three-quarters. Gun factories produce various automatic rifles, machine guns, anti-aircraft machine guns, grenade launchers, and various bullets. Its grenade launcher can also be used as a rifle. Its breech and those used by automatic rifles are very short, and the caliber is also less than 7 mm. This is to write about its unique features. The cannons produced by the cannon factory generally have a barrel length of 53 times the caliber. The shells produced by the shell factory during peacetime are entirely electroplated with lead on the surface, which does not rust and is easy to store. In addition, metallurgy factories and light metal factories are not behind other countries.

Italy, once the ancient Roman Empire during its golden age, has been languishing for more than three thousand years. Compared with our China, it can be said that both are peerless. Since Mussolini came to power in 1922, Italy, which had been weak and sick for years and going against the tide, has suddenly become one of the five powers, and recently has even shown a leading force. The reasons for this cannot be ignored. In the distant East, I have heard that Mussolini's dictatorship over the Party and the country is extreme, and he handles all affairs as he wishes. I thought that such an overwhelming approach would inevitably create enemies and accumulate resentment among the people. However, after arriving in Italy and carefully observing the hearts of the people, I realized that regardless of men, women, old, and young, they all regard Mussolini as a deity and are reluctant to call him by his name directly. Mussolini's smile is considered joyful by everyone, and Mussolini's anger is considered enraging by everyone. The joys and sorrows of the whole country are tied to one person. This is because Mussolini dedicates himself to the Party and the country, is selfless, and strives to strengthen the country. Therefore, he would rather take power by force to seek peace for the country, so he does not hesitate to humble himself to the Pope. From this, it can be seen that if one reaches the realm of "the world is for all," even if everything is dictatorial, people will still love and support them without hesitation. As for developing rural areas without favoring cities, vigorously building the country with the air force, and intensifying youth training, all have a unique vision and are related to the foundation of the country. As for the Fascist Party, it is extremely strict. The Party Army is only for Party members, and Party members are only limited to those who joined the Party from a young age and are not allowed to participate in middle age. Therefore, the Fascist Party has ruled Italy for ten years, and it is still vigorous and has no signs of corruption. According to Party records in 1934, Fascism, except for Soviet Russia, which is always at odds, has a tendency to be adopted by countries around the world. My words are rambling and I do not care if they are vulgar. I hope you will give me your advice.

With respect, I wish you well.

Yang Jie respectfully bows. (February 1st, Zhengqi Society)

Sichuan Army Launches General Offensive on Tongjiang 93

The Second Phase of the Annihilation Plan for Recovering Bazhong is Completed

He Chengjun Completes the Deployment of Military Defense and Returns to Hankou

Hankou correspondence: Since the Sichuan bandit suppression army began the second phase of its general annihilation campaign, all routes have made progress. However, due to the rugged mountain roads and the varying distances, the bandit forces are elusive, and the advance is uneven. Recently, Liu Xiang ordered a full-scale offensive on all fronts, advancing towards designated targets, and taking the recovery of Bazhong as the completion of the second phase of the plan. Once the dangerous points in the Enyang River area are recovered and Bazhong County is under the control of the National Army, Xu Bandit, unable to resist the momentum, led his main force, carrying baggage, to retreat to Tongjiang. Bazhong was then captured on the 18th by the Second Route Army Tian Songyao and the Third Route Army Li Qixiang. Thus, only Tongjiang and Nanzhang counties remain in the Red Area of northern Sichuan. Liu Xiang praised the efforts of the various armies in the annihilation campaign and telegraphed awards, ordering the First Route Army to attack Mumen, open the northern road, and contact the Second, Third, Fifth, and Sixth Routes to take Tongjiang directly, setting a deadline for the capture. However, Xu Bandit has built many solid fortifications in Tongjiang, and his main force is concentrated here, so he is bound to put up a final stubborn resistance. It is expected that the National Army's annihilation campaign will have even more fierce battles. Liu Xiang recently sent a telegram to Hankou, reporting the progress of the battle to the Wuchang Headquarters and the Hankou Pacification Headquarters, stating that Xu Bandit, Chen Changhao, and others, due to their inability to support themselves, once held a meeting to decide to concentrate all their strength and launch a fierce attack on our Fifth Route Army, hoping to break through the encirclement and flee to the Kuiwan River area of Sichuan and Hubei. Unexpectedly, the attacks over two weeks were all defeated, and the foundation of the Soviet area was shaken. The bandits, struggling to cope, moved important resources to Tongjiang. The elite of the bandits have been wiped out by more than half, and their forces have been dispersed, making it easy to annihilate them. It is said that the bandits are trying to hold Tongjiang to maintain their power in Sichuan, and are also preparing to harass the border areas of Shaanxi, Hubei, and Henan. The four famous local bandits in Henan Province, Wang You, Xiao Liushao, Gu Desheng, and Yang Xiaohei, have recently been incited by the bandits to unite in southern Henan and attempt to flee to northern Hubei as the vanguard of the bandits. Wang, Xiao, Yang, and Gu have a strength of no less than 4,000 people, and are familiar with the terrain, which is enough to disrupt the National Army's line. Therefore, Xu Bandit is eager to take advantage of them. However, Wang You's force has recently been completely eliminated by the National Army. Wang Bandit himself only managed to escape with his life. Yang Xiaohei's force was also eliminated after Wang's force, and Yang was captured alive by the National Army. Xiao and Gu have only a few hundred people and can hardly survive. Therefore, Xu Bandit's plan to build a new stronghold has suffered an initial blow. As for the defense of northern Hubei, He Chengjun has completed the deployment. He stayed in Xiangfan for six days, inspecting the garrison troops, inspecting the bunker projects, and instructing the generals on the measures to prevent Xu Bandit. He was very busy. Now that the deployment has been completed, he ended his trip to Yunyang and started his return to Hankou from Fancheng on the afternoon of the 21st. He is scheduled to inspect the local garrison troops in Zaoyang, Suixian, Yingshan, and Anlu, and will not arrive in Hankou until the 23rd. He will then prepare a fundamental plan to suppress the bandits and telegraph it to Chairman Chiang for approval. (21st)

Shandong Provincial Army Launches Large-Scale Encirclement and Annihilation of Liu Bandit 94

More Than 20,000 Troops and Militiamen Mobilized

More Than 1,000 of Liu's Bandits are Surrounded in Yuncheng

Jinan correspondence: Liu Guitang's forces were divided into two groups, attempting to flee to the Yuncheng area. The armies are intercepting them separately. Gu Liangmin, commander of the 22nd Division, has moved from Jining to Juye to command. Sun Tongxuan, commander of the 20th Division and commander of the Lunan Garrison, is commanding everything in Yanzhou. According to reports, Liu's forces total more than 2,000 people, with 21 machine guns, 8 mortars, and 1 radio. However, ammunition is very scarce. Handgun bullets are the most, but each gun has less than 100 rounds, so they dare not open fire with the government army. The telephone line between Dingtao and Cao County was cut by Liu's forces on the 18th and restored on the 19th. Han Fuju, Chairman of the Provincial Government, originally planned to go to Yanzhou early on the 19th to command, but the situation eased, so he temporarily suspended the plan. The special train is still stationed, waiting for orders. Fearing that Liu's forces would cross the Jinpu Railway to the east via the Dawenkou area and return to the old nest in the mountains of southern Shandong, Han ordered Zhan Shutang, commander of the 80th Division, to lead the directly subordinate battalions and companies and Tang Bangzhi's 241st Brigade to open up the Dawenkou Nanyi area for defense. Dai Hongbin, commander of the armored train, took three armored trains to patrol back and forth between Tai'an and Lincheng to prevent Liu's forces from destroying the railway. The Ma Guanyi Brigade of the 74th Division stationed in Dezhou had already passed through Jinan on the 19th. Han Fuju often used the phone to command the armies, and said that if Liu's forces passed through the defense zone and the officers and soldiers were not injured, it would be due to ineffective interception and annihilation, and they should be held responsible.

Also, according to reports from the front, it is said that Liu's forces of more than 1,000 people fled from Henan to Zhongdi Quan, 18 li southwest of Cao County on the morning of the 17th. In the afternoon, they were severely attacked by Wu Yuanxing's regiment of the 58th Brigade of the 20th Division, Liu Ying's third-way militia regiment of Gu Liangyou's forces, and the Cao County militia. When they tried to flee back to Henan, Tan Zixin's cavalry chased them from behind. In desperation, they fled north to Weiwanji, 35 li west of Cao County on the 18th. Wu Yuanxing's regiment followed and chased north. The first and second battalions of Gu Liangyou's militia regiment in Zhuanmiao were coming from the north, and both sides attacked in unison. In this battle, more than 200 of Liu's forces were killed. At night, Liu's forces fled east through Guyingji, west of Chengwu County, turned north, and passed between Rangouji, southeast of Dingtao County, and Chenji, northeast of Dingtao County. On the 19th, they were intercepted by Li Xuande's cavalry regiment and the Dingtao militia brigade. They then fled northeast and arrived at Taipingji, 60 li west of Juye County on the evening of the same day. This morning (20th), they were surrounded and attacked on all sides by Wu Yuanxing's regiment, Lin Binghai's regiment of the 22nd Division, Li Yide's cavalry regiment, and Gu Liangyou's militia regiment. The fighting was fierce. It is estimated that more than 200 of Liu's forces were killed, more than 300 horses were killed, more than 100 people were captured alive, and more than 100 guns were captured. Liu's elite forces were almost completely lost. The remaining remnants of 6-700 people fled to the northwest of Yuncheng this afternoon (20th). Tonight, the armies are encircling them from all sides from Jiaxiang, Juye, Shouzhang, Caozhou, and Wenshang. The government army, together with Gu Liangyou, Xie Changxian, and the militia regiments on each route, totals about 20,000 people. Liu's forces have really run out of options. The Yellow River is to the northwest of Yuncheng, and the Grand Canal is to the northeast. They are trapped in the horns, and the south is densely covered with troops. The government has long since sailed away the boats on the Yellow River and the Grand Canal, intending to annihilate Liu's forces there. Liu's forces cannot advance or retreat. It is expected that they will be eliminated within a few days. Liangshan, where Song Jiang and others were entrenched, is located in Yuncheng. The government, fearing that Liu's forces would flee there, has also sent heavy troops to guard it. (March 20th)

Northern Fujian Bandit Suppression Army Closes in on the Bandit Area on the Jiangxi Border 95

—Taining Recovered, Royal Troops Stationed in Taining City—

—The Red Bandits are Already Trapped in a Four-Sided Encirclement—

Fuzhou correspondence: According to a telegram from the 10th Column Headquarters received by the Fuzhou Provisional Headquarters on the 20th, Taining County was recovered by Wang Zhonglian's division on the afternoon of the 19th. The bandit puppet 7th Army Group retreated into Jianning. Wang's troops seized 2 heavy machine guns, more than 300 rifles, captured more than 200 bandit officers and soldiers, wounded one puppet division commander, killed two puppet battalion commanders, and wounded or killed more than 300 bandit soldiers. Wang's troops have stationed themselves in Taining City, sending teams to search for bandit traces in the villages and handle local relief. However, a group of local Red bandits, Zou Qi's force, numbering about 1,000 people, took advantage of the fierce fighting on the Fujian-Jiangxi border to wreak havoc between Chong'an and Pucheng counties. Yesterday, the Provisional Headquarters ordered Liu Heding, commander of the 9th Column, to quickly send Zhang Luanji's division, stationed in Pucheng, to carry out the annihilation campaign. As for the entire military affairs of bandit suppression in northern Fujian, Chairman Chiang originally ordered Wei Lihuang, commander of the Eastern Route Front, to preside over it. However, after Wei arrived in the province from Quanzhou, his old rib pain recurred, and he requested a month's leave to recuperate in the province. Recently, the military progress in northern Fujian has been extremely rapid, and it is essential to have a dedicated commander. A telegram was sent to Wei urging him to go to supervise the battle immediately. The Red bandits on the Fujian border are already trapped in a four-sided encirclement. The bandit areas only remain in Jianning, Ninghua, Changting, and Liancheng counties. The date of their elimination should not be far off. (March 21st)

Xiamen Wealthy Merchant Zeng Shangyuan Kidnapped 96

Boat Crossing the Sea Missing

No News for Four Days

Xiamen correspondence: Zeng Shangyuan, a wealthy Xiamen merchant who returned from Yangon, was kidnapped by someone on the night of the 17th while crossing to Gulangyu by private motorboat. The boat is missing. An empty boat was found on Dongyu the next day. As of today (21st), there is still no news. This is an unprecedented major kidnapping case in Xiamen. There are many wealthy overseas Chinese who have returned to Xiamen, but this is the first time someone has been kidnapped. The process is as follows:

Zeng Shangyuan is from Tong'an, an overseas Chinese from Yangon, 65 years old, and runs a business in Southeast Asia. He once served as the general manager of the Singapore Overseas Chinese Bank and is currently still the chairman of the bank's board of directors. He returned to China ten years ago and has a huge fortune. He invested in real estate development in Xiamen's municipal reform, and built a row of huge mansions on Datong Road, next to the customs, which also serve as the Daqian Hotel and Restaurant. He lives at 38 Anhaijiao, Gulangyu. He must come to Xiamen every day to observe the business. Although Zeng is a wealthy man, he is very frugal. He usually crosses the sea by small boat. Recently, he purchased a private motorboat from Linsen Company for crossing the sea early and late. At 9:00 PM on the 17th, Zeng left the Daqian Hotel and crossed the sea by private motorboat. Unexpectedly, late at night, the family saw that Zeng had not returned and called Daqian to inquire. They replied that he had returned. They urgently sent someone to inquire at the wharves and relatives' homes on Gulangyu, but there was no trace of him, and the motorboat was also gone. By the morning of the next day (18th), there was still no news. Zeng's son, Yangwang, reported the case to the Maritime Branch Security Bureau, the Xiamen Public Security Bureau, and the Eastern Route Headquarters sent personnel to investigate. He also hired Luanji Electric Boat to search the nearby sea. At about 4:00 PM, the Maritime Public Security Bureau received a report from Li Minghua and Li Yuji, the heads of Dongyu Village, across the sea from Xiamen, stating that an unmarked motorboat was found drifting near the coast of Dongyu in the morning of the 18th, without anyone driving it. They did not know who had lost it. In addition to sending a guard team to temporarily guard it, they requested that personnel be dispatched quickly to investigate. On the morning of the 19th, the Maritime Public Security Bureau dispatched personnel along with Zeng's family to Dongyu to inspect it. It was indeed the motorboat Zeng was riding in. Many white lime powders were found in the boat, and the carpets in the boat were very messy, as if the bandits and Zeng had a struggle. There was a bullet hole on the right side of the wooden side of the bow steering room, and the window glass was shattered. A Browning shell casing was left on the ground. Judging from this, the bullet seemed to have been fired from inside the boat, so the shell casing was left in the boat. However, no blood was seen. In addition to Zeng, the helmsman Lin Tianguo and the driver Xu Hanguo were also missing. After this case occurred, all the detectives from the Land and Maritime Public Security Bureau urgently investigated. According to reports late on the 19th, there were more than 20 bandits who kidnapped Zeng, with eight Mauser pistols and two Thompson submachine guns, using three sailboats to carry out the kidnapping. The boats were still in the Houneicao area behind Gulangyu and would soon be heading elsewhere. The Maritime Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched more than 20 armed police officers on two electric boats, but found nothing upon arrival. Daqian Hotel presented a petition to the Eastern Route Headquarters, requesting that they be ordered to solve the case quickly. Zeng's son, Yangwang, also presented a petition to the Overseas Chinese Association, requesting that they forward it to the authorities for rescue. The Overseas Chinese Association immediately forwarded it. As of the night of the 20th, according to Zeng's family, there was still no news, and they had not received a letter from the bandits. According to Daqian Hotel's news, two bandits had stayed at Daqian Hotel a week before. When Zeng went to the hotel every day, they talked to Zeng and were already acquainted with each other. On the night of the 17th, the two invited Zeng to dinner and then said they were going to Gulangyu. Zeng invited them to take the motorboat together, and the two replied that it was very good. They then took the motorboat together. It is suspected that Zeng was kidnapped by them. (March 21st)

Summary of General Resolutions of Provincial Administrative Conference 97

Nine Items Including Provincial Financial and Judicial Systems

The Provisional Headquarters Issues a Circular to All Provinces for Conscientious Implementation

Nanchang correspondence: After the Administrative Conference of Eleven Provinces opened in the auditorium of the Provisional Headquarters on the 18th, the first general assembly was held in the morning. Chairman Chiang gave a speech, and the provinces reported on their political situations separately. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM. From 2:00 PM to 7:00 PM in the afternoon, the reports continued. At 9:00 AM on the 19th, an expanded memorial week was held. A total of more than 600 people attended, including the officials attending the conference from the eleven provinces and all the attendees from the Provisional Headquarters. Chairman Chiang gave a speech for three hours, mainly on the idea that doing things must start with small things, and governing soldiers and teaching the people should start with simple things, doing things in an orderly and unified manner. Since ancient times, literati have had to know military preparedness, especially during this period of bandit suppression. Military affairs and politics should be integrated. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM. All members of the General Assembly and senior officials of the Provisional Headquarters went to a public banquet held by the Provincial Government. Chairman Xiong delivered a welcome speech and reported on the bandit suppression situation in the province. From 2:00 PM to 7:00 PM, the third general assembly was held, and the representatives of each province continued to report and propose important cases. At 9:00 AM on the 20th, the fourth general assembly was held. The administrative officials of the eleven provinces all attended. After Chairman Chiang presided over the meeting and performed the rituals, he categorized the reports from the provincial governments, the heads of the civil and educational departments, and the commissioners of the administrative districts already established in each province, and made a general criticism and corrections. First, those with special achievements were ordered to be models. Second, for those with difficulties and those that could not be done, the methods were changed to avoid obstacles. Third, those with rifts and disputes were urged to improve. Fourth, special suggestions were adopted and implemented. Fifth, shortcomings were corrected and remedied. After the reports were completed, Chiang instructed on nine important methods for refreshing politics, which served as the general resolutions of the conference. The closing ceremony was held at 12:30 PM, and each person was given a copy of Kang Ji Lu and Zi Xin Shu handwritten by Chiang. The nine methods shown are recorded below with appropriate adjustments:

(A) "Provincial Government System" (1) Unify provincial government orders to avoid disputes, and at the same time increase the power of the administrative supervision commissioners. The provincial government's orders to the counties are transferred by the commissioners. (2) Centralize the power of the provincial government. The orders of each department are decided and implemented by the provincial government. (B) "Finance" (3) Unified revenue and expenditure by the financial department. (4) Implement the collection of urban land tax to reduce the burden on farmers and enrich the national treasury. (C) "Improvement of the Judiciary" (5) All people's lawsuits must be concluded within 30 days and must not be delayed. (6) At the same time, the provincial government issues a circular to the counties regarding all pending cases and subsequent cases, which must be settled within 30 days. (D) "Drug Prohibition" (7) Issue a strict circular to conscientiously investigate and eliminate red pills, white flour, opium, and eradicate tobacco seedlings to eliminate drugs. (E) "Police Force" (8) The police should focus on quality rather than quantity, raise the salaries and status of the police, and provide education. (9) The Baojia system implements the officer area and military officer area system. The above items are issued by the Provisional Headquarters to all provinces for conscientious implementation. (20th)

Nanchang Lantern Parade 98

Promoting the New Life Movement

Over 70,000 Participants

Nanchang Correspondence: The Nanchang New Life Movement Lantern Parade was held on the 18th. Various government organizations and schools enthusiastically carried lanterns to gather at the stadium, reaching over 300 groups. The number of participants reached 70,000 to 80,000, all assembled at designated locations. After the chairman of the presidium, Deng Wenyi, performed the opening ceremony, Deng delivered a speech, stating that implementing the New Life Movement is the glory of the Chinese nation. We must tell the people of the whole country to implement the New Life Movement. Although the lanterns held by everyone today are of various shapes and colors, they are not the same; however, I believe that everyone's spirit in implementing the New Life Movement is fully expressed. I hope to maintain this spirit, and I hope everyone will act according to the intention of today. Then slogans were shouted: 1. Cultivate Propriety; 2. Know Shame; 3. Be Responsible; 4. Observe Discipline; 5. Be Punctual; 6. Love Cleanliness. After the meeting, the parade began, led by the military band, followed by the New Life Movement Promotion Association, with Deng Wenyi, Shao Hua, Cheng Shih-kuei, and others in the ranks. Following them were women's groups, government agencies, industry, commerce, and academic circles, and party headquarters at all levels, guided by Boy Scouts. Many people watched along the way.

The number of people participating in this lantern parade was more enthusiastic than the previous lantern parade promoting domestic goods, and the types of lanterns and their splendor were also better than the previous one. The following describes the good ones: (1) The Headquarters used lantern colors to form a giant tree. The trunk was the Republic of China, irrigated by the rules of the New Life Movement, and then the result of a strong country and a rich people could be achieved, taking the meaning of cultivating the foundation before the branches and leaves can be luxuriant. There were also five cars, divided into performances of clothing, food, housing, travel, and keeping time. The first car, clothing, was decorated with costumes of farmers, workers, merchants, students, and soldiers. Although the styles were different, they all showed that they should be neat and tidy. The second car, food, was decorated with a cafe, where customers explained that cold food should not be eaten. The third car, housing, was decorated with a model family, showing people an example of living facilities. The fourth car, travel, was decorated with a public road, where there were many pedestrians, but they were all in order. The fifth car, keeping time, was equipped with a giant clock, showing that time should be cherished. Each car was decorated with slogans. The cars were tied into bunkers to show people the method of guarding. (2) The Provincial Government built three platforms. One was called the life of ordinary people, where chickens and dogs lived together, the commode was placed on the bedside, and the rice pot was placed next to it. This is a sketch of the old life of ordinary people, which urgently needs to be improved. The second was the life of a fallen family, which was decorated cleanly, the clothes were simple, and the children knew etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame. Xu Zhanyuan's children, the captain of the provincial government's guard, sang the New Life Movement song on it. (3) The Highway Department had a total of eight cars. The first four cars were performances of clothing, food, housing, and travel. The fifth car was the order of the highway, the sixth car was the state of the highways in the province, the seventh car was a clock, and the eighth car was a majestic lion with shining eyes, roaring like thunder, named the Awakening Lion, implying the meaning of awakening the people of the country quickly. Also, on the top of the fourth car, there was a small car with exquisite decoration, which attracted attention. (4) Various groups, the bank sector made a brand lamp, which read "Filial Piety, Brotherhood, Loyalty, Trustworthiness, Propriety, Righteousness, Integrity, and Shame." Under each word, there were illustrations, which were quite essential. The Lead Printing Workers' Union and the Brush Printing Industry Workers' Union both used white cloth, supporting the face, filled with lights in the middle, looking like a dragon lantern from a distance, and covered with slogans when viewed, and printed cartoons of the New Life Movement, which were distributed everywhere for publicity. The Salt Stacking Workers' Union used more than ten horses, decorated with figures, all kinds of new-style modern, old-style villages, and various costumes, all of which were available, and many implications were worth adopting. The Cloth Industry Guild used various colors of local cloth to make lanterns, which also conformed to the purpose of simplicity. The Firecracker Industry had a platform for Mencius' mother teaching her son, and the Drama Industry had dramas of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, and love, all of which had profound meanings. (5) Schools: The lanterns of various primary and secondary schools were mostly in the form of New Life Movement symbols, and occasionally one or two made fly-swatting lanterns and garbage-sweeping lanterns. However, the ranks of Boy Scouts and Girl Scouts from all walks of life were neat, shouting slogans, singing New Life Movement songs, and the order was orderly, which was better than the industrial and commercial sectors. (6) Shops: The lanterns participated in by various shops mostly contained advertising effects. (Datong Society, March 20)

Songjiang

Continued Record of the Great Fire at Kuatang Bridge 99

The fire at Ren Runyuan's house in Kuatang Bridge the night before last spread to many houses, as reported in this newspaper. According to local people who witnessed it, three days before the fire, a black dog jumped from Kuatang Bridge onto the roof of a certain surname, went east, jumped over the lane to the roof of Ren Runyuan's house, barked wildly, and then went down. Also, two days before this fire, Zhang Chunyu's son, who was affected by the fire, ran from the roof for no reason and jumped over the lane. His family was shocked and followed him, saying that the house had been stolen, but in fact it was safe and sound. Usually he was not crazy, but suddenly this happened. It is said that it was an omen before the fire.

Haimen

Seizure of a Large Batch of Red Pill Raw Materials 100

Zhang Shunfu, a native of this county, carried a large batch of coffee essence (one of the raw materials for red pills) in Shanghai the day before yesterday, intending to take a boat to Haimen. He was seized by the Water Patrol Team of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau at the Xirenhe Wharf in the South City. Both the person and the stolen goods were transferred to the local court for interrogation. According to Zhang's confession, this batch of medicinal materials was entrusted by his friend Jin Shaochang to be delivered to the Zhongying Pharmacy in Haimen County for use in combination with medicines, denying that it was a raw material for making red pills. The local court believed that it was necessary to thoroughly investigate whether this batch of medicinal materials was used for making red pills, so it sent a letter to the county government of this county, ordering the police to search the pharmacy. The county government secretly ordered the County Public Security Bureau yesterday (the 19th). The section chief Xu Wenlong and inspector Ding Zuozhou led more than ten armed police officers to search. They found eight iron boxes of coffee essence and more than ten pieces of scattered pill materials such as sugar powder and Taikoo sugar. They took the owner of the store, Pu Zhuping, to the bureau and sent him to the county government for interrogation the next day.

Wuxi

Public Appeal to Preserve Ancient Tombs of the Ming Dynasty 106

In You Duli, 18th ward outside the East Gate, formerly known as Huixi, there is an ancient tomb of the You family, which is recorded in the county chronicles. There are five people in the tomb: (1) You Jujing, a commoner of the Ming Dynasty, gifted the title of associate administrator; (2) You Wupu, repeatedly solicited for filial piety and integrity in Yongle Jihai, Xuande Kuichou, and Zhengtong Dingyi, assisted in the seventh rank, served as a great guest of the township drink, and was enshrined in the township sage shrine of this county; (3) You Zhengyan, a Juren in Jingtai Gengwu, the magistrate of Suian County, Zhejiang, and the associate administrator of Yongchang; (4) You Shiqian was recommended to serve as an instructor in Wujin County; (5) You Suiliang, a Juren in Chenghua Kuimao, served as the magistrate of Chuxiong, Chongyang, Cangwu, and Jiangchuan counties, and was enshrined in the famous officials shrines of Yunnan and Guangxi provinces. Gong Wupu wrote two volumes of quotations, which can be found in the History of the Ming Dynasty and the Collection of the Tenth Beginning, which can be found in the Bibliography of Xishan Dynasties. Gong Suiliang wrote the Draft of Political Affairs and the Draft of Living at Home, which can be found in the Bibliography of Xishan Dynasties. You Jujing was born in the fourth month of the third year of the Yuan Dynasty. He was ordered by the imperial court to cultivate ten hectares of land, and he opened a pool in the gap land and obtained thirty ingots of medium gold to help the villagers. The villagers praised his virtue, so they changed the name Huixi to You Tu (now called You Duli) to show that they would not forget. It can be seen that he was a famous sage at that time. At that time, Gong Wupu had submitted memorials to the Ministry of Personnel, etc., calling him a true Confucian scholar of the holy world, all of which are recorded in the county chronicles and the Changzhou prefectural chronicles. Recently, the Xihu Highway was built, and its route happened to include the tomb. After hearing the news, his descendant You Tong (Gan Cheng) said that the tomb had a historical relationship and was recorded in the county chronicles. There were only 26 famous tombs in the Ming Dynasty, and the You family actually occupied two of them. He could not bear to destroy the ancient tomb of the famous sage. On the 15th and 19th of this month, he telegraphed Shen, the director of the Construction Department, asking the county to bypass the tomb. After the telegram was sent, he did not receive a reply, so he submitted another presentation yesterday, detailing the process. The text briefly investigates and handles road work. Whenever encountering the tomb of a famous person, unless it is absolutely necessary, it is usually bypassed. Moreover, according to the method told by Director Zhang of the Construction Bureau, the shift is only dozens of feet, which has nothing to do with the overall situation. Moving the tomb to the plain is just a matter of raising a hand, and the ancient tomb of the famous sage can be preserved, which is a great blessing. It is now heard that the project will start soon, and I respectfully ask for a quick decision and a clear instruction. The dead will be grateful underground, and the living will be grateful for generations to come. It is also heard that more than ten gentry of the county, including Cai Wenxin, have also jointly submitted a presentation to Director Shen, asking to slightly change the route of the road, only needing to go straight to the route on the north side of Youdu River, after the Xiao Lane and on the roadbed of the Backpack Lane, which can be straightened and save the construction of a bridge, which is beneficial to both the public and private sectors. It is thought that Director Shen will definitely adopt it.

Qingjiang

Recent Situation of the Liutang River Dredging Project 108

In the past, the Liutang River Project in Jiangbei was in disrepair for a long time, so whenever there was a year of flooding or a mountain torrent, the farmland in the seven counties along the river, including Suqian, Siyang, Huaiyin, Shuyang, Lianshui, and Dongguan, would be flooded. Shen Baixian, the current director of the Jiangsu Construction Department, moved to dredge the river in all directions when he was the director of the Construction Department, but it did not come to fruition. Last year, when Shen first took office, he continued to proceed and was finally approved by the provincial government meeting, and Xu Dingkang, the director of the Transportation Bureau, was commissioned to concurrently serve as the director of the project. It has been three months, according to recent surveys, Shuyang should do the most engineering, totaling 800,000 cubic meters of earthwork, and County Magistrate Shen Jinghua is still able to be loyal to his duties, recruiting more than 14,000 workers every day, stationed in the work area to supervise, and the embankment project will be completed by the end of the month, and the dredging work will also be started after preliminary testing, and it can be completed in about less than May. Suqian, Lianshui, and Donghai counties have each allocated 400,000 cubic meters of earthwork, except for Donghai County Magistrate Wen Qinming, who was dismissed for negligence, Suqian County Magistrate Zhang Naifan and Lianshui County Magistrate Yang Tongsheng are all able to fulfill their duties and can be completed within April. Guanyun is located in the lower reaches of Liutang, and the river center of the Longgou and other places in the territory is silted up, making dredging difficult, and its county magistrate was also dismissed for negligence. It is difficult to reverse the construction period until the new county magistrate takes office. Siyang has allocated 100,000 more cubic meters of earthwork than Guanyun, totaling 350,000, and the number of workers arriving every day is about 4,000, and it can be completed after the middle of next month. Among the seven counties, Huaiyin has only allocated 130,000 cubic meters of earthwork, the smallest number, but there are more than 1,000 workers arriving every day, and it can also be completed within this month.

After the meeting, representatives from the newspapers went to the county government and the county party headquarters to petition. County Magistrate Dai and Standing Committee Member Gu received them and gave satisfactory answers to the first item of the resolution and decided to investigate and severely punish the perpetrators.
