Local News

Central Executive Committee Explains Penalties for Publishing Law 116

And Informs National Government to Order Courts to Comply

Xinxin News Agency, Beijing: The Central Executive Committee previously received a presentation from the Shanghai Newspaper Guild requesting an explanation of whether newspaper editors or publishers should be dealt with in accordance with the penalties of the Publishing Law when they are sued for publishing news. The Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee submitted the case to the Standing Committee for approval and replied to the Guild. The Shanghai Newspaper Guild's presentation and the Central Executive Committee's reply are recorded below:

Editor and Publisher Sued for Publishing News: Presentation requesting instructions on whether newspaper editors or publishers should be dealt with in accordance with the penalties of the Publishing Law when they are sued for publishing news. The presenter believes that newspaper editors and publishers collect and record news as third parties. Even if the original manuscript contains excesses beyond the scope of facts and violates civil and criminal laws or other regulations, the editor or publisher has no initial intention to commit an offense and has no persistent malice. The legal responsibility they should bear is, at most, within the scope of negligence and cannot be regarded as intentional. Therefore, except for the serious circumstances specified in Article 19 of the Publishing Law, which should be punished in accordance with Article 35 of the same law, other circumstances are relatively minor and should be corrected by publishing corrections or rebuttals in accordance with Article 14 of the same law. Other laws should not be cited for sanctions against editors and publishers who are purely third parties. The Secretariat of the Union clearly explained this in its reply to the Civil Service Office of the National Government, Secret Letter No. 14298. However, in recent times, law enforcers have often ignored this explanation of the Union and have not examined the intent of the accused party, but have punished the author, editor, and publisher in accordance with civil and criminal laws or other regulations, causing the editors and publishers of newspapers to lose the protection they should have under the Publishing Law, and confusing the author's intentional actions with the editor and publisher's negligence, which is obviously unfair and violates the spirit of the law, making those who operate newspapers feel insecure. Therefore, the presenter is specially requesting the Union to review and approve a clear explanation order for compliance in order to end disputes and ensure the safety of the newspaper industry, which is not only the prayer of the presenter, but also the intention of the Central Government to maintain the newspaper industry. Respectfully presented to the Central Executive Committee.

Deal with it in accordance with the Publishing Law, not with other methods: Regarding the case presented by your Guild requesting an explanation of whether newspaper editors or publishers should be dealt with in accordance with the penalties of the Publishing Law when they are sued for publishing news, the Standing Committee approved, "Check the case and reply," stating that newspaper agencies and news agencies are established after applying for registration in accordance with the procedures of the Publishing Law. Therefore, unless the editor of a newspaper violates the provisions of ordinary civil and criminal laws due to personal actions, or violates the restrictions of Article 19 of the Publishing Law, and can be punished in accordance with the provisions of Article 35 of the same law in accordance with other heavier laws, for all other violations of the Publishing Law, courts at all levels should deal with it in accordance with the provisions of the Publishing Law and should not cite other laws for sanctions. This explanation has been transferred to the National Government to inform courts at all levels to comply with it and to inform the Ministry of the Interior. In view of the above, this reply is hereby made for your information. To the Shanghai Newspaper Guild, Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee.

The Ministry of Finance is Actively Carrying out the Reorganization of National Land Tax 121

A meeting is scheduled to be convened in May

Earnestly discuss the reorganization method

Xinxin News Agency reports that in order to reorganize the land tax and abolish various exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous taxes and relieve the burden on the people, Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Finance, once drafted measures to reorganize the land tax and abolish exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous taxes, which were submitted to the Fourth Plenary Session for approval. Xinxin News Agency reporters learned from the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Finance that Kong plans to convene provincial and municipal financial authorities to a meeting in Beijing in May of this year in order to actively carry out the reorganization.

Earnest Consultation: It is found that there are many kinds of taxes and levies in various provinces, cities, and counties, and each has a certain purpose. How should they be separately deleted and reorganized by the local government? It is necessary for the central government and local financial authorities to earnestly consult and plan as a whole before a decision can be made on the implementation method. It is also learned that the Ministry of Finance has now established a preparatory office for the financial conference, and will discuss the scope of this discussion and various

Item rules, will be drafted immediately.

Implementation Method: The implementation methods to be formulated by the Ministry of Finance are excerpted as follows: (A) The Executive Yuan orders the provincial and municipal governments to be responsible for thoroughly investigating the names, tax rates, and uses of all taxes in each county and locality within the province and city, and to complete the investigation by March of this year. (B) The provincial and municipal governments shall, based on the results of the investigation, conduct detailed research and refer to the actual financial situation within the province and city to formulate a concrete plan to reduce the land tax surcharge and abolish exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous taxes, and complete it by May of this year. The report and plan shall be sent to the Ministry of Finance. (C) After receiving the reports and plans from the provinces and cities, the Ministry of Finance shall conduct further research and make an overall plan, and convene the financial authorities of the provinces and cities to Beijing in June of this year to hold a meeting to earnestly discuss and decide on the methods of cutting, abolishing, and offsetting, and to agree on the types and scope of local taxes, and future tax increases must go through legal procedures.

The Jianghai Customs Revises the Registration Method for Customs Declaration by Business Firms 130

Register with the Customs in accordance with the regulations starting next month

Blank application forms can be obtained from the Customs

In order to revise the registration method for customs declaration by business firms, the Jianghai Customs Commissioner has issued Announcement No. 1348, stating that the method for business firms and customs declaration firms to register with the Customs has been announced by the General Affairs Section of the Customs on January 15 of the Republic of China, 21 years. Now, the items related to the customs registration of business firms in this method are revised as follows: Starting from April 1 of this year, all domestic or foreign business firms and individuals handling customs declaration matters must register with the Customs or re-register in accordance with the following regulations: (A) The first registration application must be certified. The certification procedures are as follows: (1) If the applicant is a domestic citizen, it must be certified by a reliable merchant, business firm, or institution known to the Customs. (2) If the applicant is a foreigner with extraterritorial rights, it must be certified by the competent consul. (3) If the applicant is a foreigner without extraterritorial rights, it must be certified by a reliable merchant, business firm, or institution known to the Customs. (B) All business firms or individuals who have registered must prepare an application form in January of each year and submit it to the Customs for re-registration once. However, this application form does not need to be certified. The method for customs declaration firms to register with the Customs has not changed, and the seals and signatures submitted to the Customs for record will not be affected by this revision. Starting from April 1 of this year, if business firms and individuals have not re-registered in accordance with this revised method, they will be deemed as unregistered. Before completely handling in accordance with the revised method, the registration applications submitted will not be accepted. The annual guarantee of each shipping company will not be affected by this revision. Business firms that need this blank registration application form can obtain it from the business firm and customs declaration registration counter in the General Affairs Section of the Customs. All merchants are hereby notified. Commissioner Bolotte.

The Chamber of Commerce Requests a Reduction in the Diesel Tax Rate 131

The National Chamber of Commerce submitted a document to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance of the National Government in Nanjing yesterday, requesting a reduction in the diesel tax rate: (Titles omitted) Recently, the representatives of the member companies of the affiliated association have come to the meeting one after another, all stating that the Ministry of Finance has levied 26.3 gold units per ton of diesel oil imported since February 1 of this year, which is about 49 yuan in national currency. According to the original price of the diesel oil, which is more than 70 yuan per ton, the added tariff has reached 70% of the oil price, which is really unexpected. At this time when industry and commerce are declining, our power industry is particularly affected. If we suddenly increase this huge amount of oil tax again, business will be more difficult and will be in a desperate situation. We believe that your association is the hub of all industries in Zhejiang. Please consider the vital interests of the member companies and quickly appeal to the government to find a way to provide relief and maintain a glimmer of life. We are deeply dependent on it. It is said that the use of diesel engine power generation in the electrical companies in Zhejiang Province has accounted for 89%. At this time when the people are poor and business is difficult, the electrical industry is no exception. However, because public utilities are closely related to social stability and factory production, we have to maintain it despite the deficit. Now, the heavy tax on diesel oil has suddenly increased, which has put us in a desperate situation. Correspondingly, we hereby request your association to forward it to the government, requesting a reduction in the levy to relieve the business difficulties, etc., and to approve this. The National Chamber of Commerce kowtows.

A Wooden Ship with Sunken Wood off the Coast of Wusong Estuary 132

The wooden ship Jinyufa, loaded with wood from Fujian to Shanghai, arrived at the Xiaota ocean surface about 70 miles off the coast of Wusong Estuary at about 8:00 PM on the 20th. Between buoys No. 3 and No. 4, it suddenly encountered a violent wind and rain, and huge waves, which caused it to lose its steering ability. After being hit by several huge waves, the bottom of the ship suddenly flooded and the hull cracked. Tens of thousands of pieces of wood were lost at the same time. At that time, all the sailors climbed to the mast and sails in an attempt to escape. In an instant, the ship completely sank into the sea, and only a few feet of the tens of feet high mast were exposed above the water. At that time, a total of 19 old sailors were drowned, including sailors Zhong Aden, Jin Yi, and Wang Xinzhang, who clung to the sails and drifted with the wind. In the evening and early morning, the Ningbo Liner New Beijing arrived in Shanghai from Ningbo, and heard Zhong and others shouting for help, and then learned the previous situation. However, due to the excessive speed of the ship and the tide, it was unable to rescue them at that time. When the ship arrived in Songjiang, it notified the Wusong Maoxing Company, which immediately dispatched the Lisheng small steamer to rush to the scene of the accident. Zhong and others were rescued back to Shanghai, and three more corpses were seen drifting with the sails. It was not until yesterday morning that people from the Shanghai Timber Company hired a boat to go to inspect and find ways to salvage them. It is reported that the loss of this shipment is estimated to be more than 100,000 yuan.

In Shanghai, Zhu Dechao is in charge of everything, and is soliciting unanimous participation from various factories in the city. It is currently in active progress.

Assisting the Export Association: Since the Chicago Exposition Export Association decided to continue to participate in the 1934 Chicago Expo, it has been proceeding with all the work in separate groups because the opening date is approaching. In addition to sending letters to various provinces to collect exhibits, and because the company is a production and sales cooperation agency and has considerable contact with various manufacturers, it also sent a letter to request assistance. It is learned that the company is also sending letters to various factories to transport various excellent products to compete, as a prelude to developing foreign trade.

Setting up an Exhibition in Northwest China: The association had previously discussed the progress methods by letter between Liu Ruzhan, Director of the Gansu Construction Department, and Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce. 工部局 Considers Changing Election Procedures 136

Not Feasible This Year

During the annual taxpayers' meeting in April of last year, the Shanghai Municipal Council proposed a slight revision to Article 18 of the Land Regulations to improve the procedures for electing directors and to better suit the current situation. This revision includes four points: (1) increasing the number of polling places; (2) abolishing the procedure of voters signing their names; (3) extending the polling hours from the original 10:00 AM to 3:00 PM to 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM; and (4) increasing the number of vote counters. After the proposal was passed by the taxpayers' meeting, the Municipal Council, following established procedures, sent a letter to the leading consul on April 27, requesting them to complete the necessary procedures so that the amendment could take effect. However, the Chinese government has not yet expressed its agreement to this amendment, so the procedures have not been fully completed. The board elections this year will still be conducted according to the old rules.

A New Stop Added at Dahongqiao for Joint Transportation

It was resolved that (1) station chiefs and railway police will be responsible for maintaining order when passengers purchase tickets; (2) the opening time for ticket windows at small stations will remain as usual, opening one hour before train arrival; (3) station staff duties and regulations, and loud hawking by vendors will be specified and prohibited by the station chiefs separately. Cotton Cloth Market to Officially Open 140

Notice to Weaving Households to Expedite Production of Light-Colored Cloth for the Market

Strict Measures for Receiving Yarn to Prevent Mixing in Inferior Yarn

The China National Cotton Cloth Market on Guizhou Road in this city is actively preparing for its official opening. In order to promote the sale of domestically produced yarn, in addition to speeding up the construction of its own market to ensure early completion, the market has notified weaving households to expedite the production of light-colored cloth for market sales. Basic weaving households have also signed contracts to expedite the production of ordered goods. To prevent a few unscrupulous individuals among the weaving households from taking advantage of loopholes and mixing in inferior yarn, the market has established rules that basic weaving households receiving yarn for weaving ordered goods must receive it according to a fixed quota and not take more than they need or spend less. With these regulations, weaving households will not be able to mix in inferior yarn or illegally reduce costs, and the quality of goods will be uniform, which will benefit the purchasing of various customers. It is reported that the first phase of contracted basic weaving households in the market consists of 2,000 looms, with each loom producing one bolt of cloth per day, resulting in a monthly production of 60,000 bolts, requiring 1,500 pieces of yarn. Once the cloth market is successful, it will gradually expand to achieve the goal of controlling the Shanghai family cotton cloth industry and promoting the sale of domestically produced yarn.

Import of Headless Bulbs Taxed as Finished Products 143

Unscrupulous merchants import inferior headless bulbs as raw materials to evade taxes, and then sell them under different brands, which greatly affects the sales of domestic electric bulbs. This has attracted great attention from the electrical industry. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency interviewed Mr. Hu Xiyuan, chairman of the Electrical Appliance Manufacturing Industry Association, yesterday to inquire about the outcome of the above matter. According to Mr. Hu, since last month, the government has instructed all customs offices to collect a tariff of four yuan per day for headless bulbs, as if they were finished products. However, the unscrupulous merchants, knowing that this method of tax evasion cannot last, imported a large number of headless bulbs before the collection method was corrected. There are still many headless bulbs in stock in this city, but they have to hide them for fear of retroactive payment of tariffs.

Wu Jianguang Settles Lawsuit Against In-Laws 144

Compensation of Four Dollars for the Price of the Study Tool

Daughter Apologizes to Father-in-Law to Resolve the Matter

Wu Jianguang, a blind man, previously hired lawyer Xi Yafu to file a criminal complaint with the First Special District Court against his in-laws, Huang Fuyi, Mrs. Zhong (Huang's wife), Huang Peichu (Huang's son), and Huang's daughter, Mrs. Wu (Wu Jianguang's daughter-in-law), for damage, insult, and theft of a 50-year-old study tool. The court once summoned them and ordered them to try to settle out of court. The court also ruled that Wu Huang氏's portion was not subject to self-representation according to the law and was therefore not accepted. This has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, the case was scheduled for continued hearing. Both the plaintiff and the defendant were present. The presiding judge, Wu Xiangzu, first inquired about the settlement progress of the two parties. According to the plaintiff's agent, lawyer Xi, the two sides had begun negotiations during the adjournment, and the plaintiff had put forward two conditions: (1) The defendant was to issue a written apology; (2) The defendant was to compensate for the study tool. The defendant fully agreed to the first condition but refused to compensate for the second, resulting in the failure of the settlement. The defendant's agent, lawyer Jiang Chiping, also stated the mediation process. Judge Wu believed that the two parties were relatives and should not be involved in litigation, and that the matter was trivial. He asked the defendant, Huang Fuyi, whether he had the sincerity to settle. Huang remained silent for a long time and then said that he could only fulfill one of the two conditions. If he compensated for the study tool, he would not apologize. Subsequently, lawyer Xi persuaded Wu and proposed a solution: the defendant would compensate four yuan for the price of the study tool and express his apology in court. Both parties did not object. The defendant, Mrs. Huang Zhong, took out four yuan and gave it to Wu Jianguang, and her daughter, Mrs. Wu Huang氏 (the plaintiff's daughter-in-law), apologized to the plaintiff on behalf of the defendant. The case was then settled. After both parties signed, Judge Wu ruled that the case was not accepted.

Xujiahui Merchants and Residents Discuss Responding to the French Concession Police Crossing the Boundary to Expel Police 149

Elect Representatives to Petition the Municipal Government

Business Community Jointly Submits a Petition for Negotiation

Yesterday afternoon, shops in Xujiahui Town in western Shanghai gathered at the office of the Town's Business Community Federation to hold an emergency meeting to discuss countermeasures against the French Municipal Council's demolition of water pipes, expulsion of vendors, and deprivation of our police power, which are major events. Those present included Yang Jingcheng of Bao Kang Rice Store, Jing Yiyi of Wan Shen Sauce Garden, Dong Xueshi of Dechangshun Nanhuhuo Store, Chen Qilie of Rendetang Pharmacy, Wang Yunqing of Wan Cui Sauce Garden, Zhu Zhaorong of Wan Yong Trough Workshop, Zhou Zhaochang of Xiangtai Butcher Shop, Xu Meilong of Longxing Restaurant, Xu Guoliang of Yuanshun Salted Goods Store, Zhang Chuanquan of Hengxing Doufu Store, as well as Zhou Chengxiang, Chairman of the Business Community Federation, Xu Jiyu, Head of the French Area Defense Corps, Chen Xiaomei of the Ninth District Party Department, Jin Xihan of the District Branch, Xie Qingbai of the Yancheng Fellow Association in Shanghai, Li Mengnan of the Ninth District Soap and Drug Industry Association, Ma Zhiyao of the Vendors' Federation, and Jiang Shouzhi, a citizen representative, totaling more than 20 people.

Zhou Chengxiang was elected as chairman and reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that the road in question had always been under the jurisdiction of the Chinese authorities, with police posts set up to maintain traffic. In the spring of 1927, when the revolutionary army arrived in Shanghai, the French Municipal Council erected wooden stakes and installed barbed wire on the road to demarcate the boundary between the Chinese and French areas and prevent fleeing soldiers from entering. In 1931, the road was repaired by the Municipal Works Bureau and paved with asphalt. Subsequently, a British commercial bus from the Fourth Route turned around at the site and was prohibited from passing by the post police of the Second Station of the Sixth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau on the grounds that the land belonged to the Chinese area. This is a fact that everyone has seen and heard. Furthermore, the fort built by the French Municipal Council on the bank of the Zhaojiabang River was also seized without authorization, and the case remains unresolved to this day. Now, the French police have also pried off the lead plate of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau Sixth District Second Station guard post nailed to the electric wire pole in front of Yang Baokang Rice Store, expelled the stationed police officers, and ordered the vendors to move away. This is a loss of sovereignty and humiliation of the country. After discussion, the results were: (1) Jointly submit a petition to the authorities to lodge a strong protest with the French Consul; (2) Elect representatives to petition the Municipal Government; (3) Send letters to various organizations for united assistance; (4) Schedule a general meeting of representatives from all walks of life in Xujiahui; (5) confidential; (6) Restore the original police power; (7) The French police are not allowed to interfere with the shacks along the riverbank under Xujiahui Road. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 p.m.

Marriage Aims Not Achieved After Two Years of Marriage 151

Sun Xiu'e Sues Sun Yusheng for Impotence

Requests Divorce and Return of Dowry

—Sun Yusheng Claims He Can Have Intercourse and Requests Inspection—

Sun Yusheng, a native of Nanxiang, is currently 26 years old. On November 10, 1931, he married Sun Xiu'e (currently 24 years old), a woman from Ningbo, through a matchmaker. Now, after more than two years, Sun Xiu'e hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the civil court of the First Special District Court, requesting a divorce and demanding compensation for dowry and other expenses totaling 2,970 yuan. The reason for this is quite amusing, and is briefly described below. The plaintiff married the defendant on November 10, 1931, and has been living with him for more than two years. Although they live in the same room, they have never been separated, but she is still a virgin and has never had intercourse. The defendant admitted that he has lung disease and often coughs up blood, so he cannot have intercourse. However, medical experts say that those who suffer from lung disease, even in the second or third stage, not only do not reduce their sexual desire, but are even more sexually motivated than ordinary people. It can be seen that the defendant must have a hidden illness that prevents him from having intercourse besides lung disease. He is obviously impotent and has no qualifications for marriage at all. The plaintiff is an old-fashioned woman and is ashamed to talk about such things. However, the defendant's condition is so serious that he is like a disabled person. If it can be cured, who would not want to be cured? Now that they have been married for two years, the purpose of marriage has not been achieved, which clearly shows that his illness is incurable. In accordance with Articles 995 and 999 of the Civil Code, she requests a divorce and the return of dowry, etc. Sun Yusheng also hired lawyer Chen Jinrong to request the Special First Court Mediation Office to summon and mediate the reasons for cohabitation. Sun stopped having intercourse for two years due to his lung disease and following doctor's orders, hoping to recover. Unexpectedly, last November, Xiu'e was instigated by others and used the excuse of returning to Ningbo to leave and never return. She also took away all the clothes and other items in the box and falsely accused him of suffering from a hidden illness. Yusheng stopped having intercourse for two years due to his doctor's orders, and the period has now expired. He is now about to have intercourse. Therefore, he requests mediation for cohabitation. Yesterday morning, Judge Luo opened the civil court No. 7 to hear Sun Xiu'e's lawsuit for divorce. The plaintiff insisted that the defendant was unable to have intercourse, but Sun Yusheng denied it, saying that he could be inspected. The court ruled that the inspection would be rescheduled before further interrogation.

After Robbing a Large Sum of Money, He Specialized in Lending at Usurious Rates 152

Accomplices in the 20,000 Yuan Robbery Case

Arrested in a Teahouse

On the 4th of last month, Shen Zhuang, the Shanghai branch of Rugao Gongyu Qianzhuang, located on the upper floor of No. 11 Hengxing West Lane, 16th Pu, Nanshi, was suddenly broken into by five bandits who robbed bank notes worth 20,600 yuan. The competent first district successively captured five bandits, including Xiao Mazi Zhou Huansheng and Qi Lingen (aka Huo Sun Lingen), who confessed that the mastermind was the company's cook, Zhou Xiaotao. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. The day before yesterday, Lu Ying, captain of the detective team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, suddenly received a tip from a confidential informant that one of the bandits in the case, Ji Bingrong, had distributed the stolen money to acquaintances such as small vendors and coolies in the area of Fangbang Bridge and the Republic Theater at usurious rates, hoping to profit from the interest. Zhou Peisan and Pan Huanzhang, officers of the team, were immediately dispatched to secretly wait at a small teahouse next to the Republic Theater. Before long, Ji, the thief, came swaggering in and took the usurious money from a barber. They immediately rushed forward and arrested him and took him back to the team. During the preliminary hearing by Captain Lu, Ji confessed that his other name was Tianlong, 43 years old, from Wujin, and lived at No. 12 Rongxiang Lane, Songxue Street, in the city. He was originally a tailor. However, he completely denied his involvement in the case. The captain ordered the thief to confront Xiao Mazi and others who had been captured in the first district. Zhou, the thief, identified Ji Bingrong, also known as A Si, as having been invited by Yang Mingchang, the mastermind who was on the run, to rob the bank. When Zhou and others broke into Guangfeng Company, Ji and Xiao Mazi went upstairs together and went straight into Gongyu Qianzhuang. Zhou also forced the victim to hand over the key to open the silver box and rob the banknotes. Ji stood next to him and threatened them with a gun. When Ji was questioned again, the thief bowed his head and said nothing. Since the matter was important, he was ordered to prepare a document and send Ji, the captured thief, to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation yesterday morning. On the other hand, he ordered his subordinates to arrest the mastermind Zhou Xiaotao and the bandit leader Yang Mingchang, who were on the run, and bring them to justice.

Case of Landlord Killed by Tenant for Rent 153

Murderer Li Zhongxian Admits to Killing

Concluding Arguments Yesterday, Awaiting Sentencing

Rong Laosan, a resident of No. 94 Zihua Road, Jiu Mu Di, and a native of Menghe, was stabbed to death by his tenant, Li Zhongxian, on the night of the 23rd of the twelfth lunar month last year for demanding rent without success. The patrol police arrested the murderer and sent him to the police station of the First Station of the Second District and then transferred him to the local court for interrogation and detention. After examination, it was confirmed that Rong Laosan died from knife wounds. The prosecutor's confession was true, and the case was prosecuted to the criminal court. The case was heard yesterday by Judge Luo Renji. First, Rong Jia氏, the wife of the deceased, testified that she was 37 years old and had one son and two daughters, all of whom were young. Her husband, Rong Laosan, was stabbed to death by Li Zhongxian. She requested justice. Her right-hand fingers were also stabbed when she went forward to seize the murder weapon. Even her ring finger and little finger were broken. Next, witness Chen Yonglin testified that he opened a redwood workshop at No. 94 and rented a one-story building to Rong Laosan for 12 yuan per month. Rong then sublet the mezzanine to Li Zhongxian. On the day of the incident, he had already gone to bed. Later, he heard screams for help upstairs. He put on his clothes and rushed upstairs and saw that Rong was dead. Li rushed out the door and ran downstairs. Because he saw Li holding the murder weapon, he did not dare to grab him. He followed him downstairs. The police knocked on the door outside. When he opened the door, Li was arrested by the police and the murder weapon was seized. Next, the murderer Li Zhongxian testified that he was from Shandong, 23 years old, and that he killed him and was not wronged. At this point, lawyer Zhou Yu defended the defendant and asked for leniency. The judge believed that the arguments were concluded and awaited sentencing. Li Zhongxian was returned to custody.

Tax Bureau Clerk Wang Mu Ran Over and Killed by a Car Yesterday 154

Wang Mu, a clerk in the General Affairs Section of the Ministry of Finance's Tax Bureau, a native of Shaoxing, Zhejiang, 58 years old, has worked in the tax bureau for ten years and is highly regarded by his superiors. Yesterday afternoon, at around 1:00 p.m., Wang walked to the intersection of Xiafei Road and Songshan Road after lunch at home to take the No. 4 tram back to the bureau to work. Unexpectedly, a car suddenly came speeding towards him. Wang was unable to avoid it and was knocked to the ground, suffering severe injuries to his waist. The Chinese police officer on duty at the station arrived, recorded the license plate number of the car that caused the accident, and hired a car to send the injured to Renji Hospital for treatment. However, due to the severity of his injuries, he died immediately upon arrival at the hospital. Colleagues in the tax bureau were saddened to hear the news.

Request from the International Cultural Research Society for Subsidies from the Sino-Belgian Boxer Indemnity Fund 155

Request for subsidies to edit the book "Belgium"

The International Cultural Research Society of this city sent a letter yesterday to the Sino-Belgian Boxer Indemnity Committee, stating: "Respectfully submitted, the diplomatic relations between China and Belgium have always been extremely cordial, and the cultural cooperation between the two countries is particularly well-known in the world. Chinese students studying in Belgium every year follow one after another, resulting in a constant stream of talented individuals. Most of them are dedicated to Sino-Belgian endeavors, and the relationship between the two countries is becoming increasingly close. To show its goodwill, Belgium uses a large portion of its returned Boxer Indemnity to engage in cultural and educational undertakings between the two countries, which is managed by your esteemed committee. The members of your esteemed committee, with their broad vision and balanced judgment, are deeply appreciated by all Chinese people. We believe that in order to promote cultural undertakings, publications are necessary for practical communication. Although there are many Chinese students studying in Belgium, very few are dedicated to this field. As a result, the so-called cultural cooperation is only one-sided and not widespread. We have been engaged in publishing for more than ten years and have considerable experience. Recognizing this, we have undertaken the editing of a book entitled "Belgium," which collects as much information as possible on various aspects, such as Belgian politics, education, customs, social practices, study abroad conditions, travel guides, etc., all of which are written into special chapters to contribute to the Chinese people. On the one hand, it will allow the Chinese people to understand the actual situation of Belgium, and at the same time, it will allow future students studying in Belgium to follow the map and obtain what they learn from, which will be of great convenience. Your esteemed committee provides many subsidies for various cultural undertakings of the Chinese people, and you must be optimistic about the success of this kind of publication that practically communicates the culture of the two countries. Moreover, we have heard that the principle of your committee's subsidies is limited to those containing Sino-Belgian relations. This kind of publication is closely related to both China and Belgium and is very much in line with the principle of requesting subsidies. Therefore, we venture to request your esteemed committee to allocate subsidies as funds for the publication of this book, so that after the publication of this book, it can be distributed to various places at home and abroad to engage in the actual promotion of Sino-Belgian culture, which will definitely be of considerable benefit. Then not only will the colleagues be grateful, but the cultural future of China and Belgium will truly benefit from it. Enclosed is the entire book's content and the method of compilation, printing, and claiming funds, as shown on the left. We respectfully request your review and reply." Sincerely, International Cultural Research Society.

Temporary meeting held yesterday

Nominating reorganization committee members

The Chinese Women's Suffrage Association held a temporary meeting at the YMCA on Sichuan Road at twelve noon yesterday to discuss expanding the organization into the Chinese Women's Movement Alliance. Fifteen members of the reorganization committee were immediately nominated. The details are as follows:

Attending Members: More than 20 members attended, including Wang Liming, Qian Jianqiu, Liu Jichen, Li Caixia, Yang Meizhen, Tang Jiawei, Zhu Baoliang, Wang Ruizhu, Xu Danzhi, Hong Jianxia, etc. Wang Liming was immediately nominated as chairman, and Liu Jichen as secretary.

Chairman's Report: Chairman Wang Liming first gave a report, stating briefly: "This association was organized in response to the Beijing Women's Suffrage Association and was established in the tenth year of the Republic of China. The purpose at that time was to obtain women's suffrage. Today, women have the opportunity to participate in politics, which is the result of the association's efforts. Now that we have obtained suffrage, women's education, occupational family issues, and other issues still require us to strengthen the solidarity of women. Looking back at the women's community in our country, there is no solidarity, which is very distressing. Therefore, this association really needs to expand its organization, unite women across the country, and promote the development of the women's movement."

Discussion of Important Cases: Next, the motions were discussed. Wang Liming proposed to change the name of the association to the Chinese Women's Movement Alliance, which was resolved and passed. The New New Company's Gatekeeper Zhou Zhanyuan's Case of Shooting and Killing Li Minzhou Mentioned Above 157

The Police Believe Zhou Killed Li with Premeditation

Request to Abolish the Original Sentence of Zhou to Capital Punishment

Zhou Zhanyuan from Tianjin had been working as the deputy head of the gatekeeper at the New New Company on Guizhou Road for eight years. He was dismissed by Li Minzhou, the general manager of the company, on February 1st of this year due to a mistake in his work. Zhou harbored resentment and, at 5:15 p.m. on the same day, took advantage of Li going to room 327 of the New New Hotel to take a bath. He hid a pistol, broke into the room, fired a shot, and hit Li's vital point, causing him to die immediately. Zhou also took the opportunity to escape, fleeing to the Guohua Branch on Beijing Road, where he asked the gatekeeper No. 2139 to borrow travel expenses, intending to flee to the puppet Manchuria. The gatekeeper reported to the police station, and he was arrested and sent to the First Special Court, which sentenced Zhou to life imprisonment for the crime of murder. Since the judgment of this case, the police believe that the original trial did not sentence him to death for premeditated murder, which is not appropriate. Therefore, the police lawyer Gan Jingxian filed an appeal with the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court. The grounds for the appeal listed the defendant's character, the reason for the dismissal, the course of the murder, the preparation for the murder, and the reasons for the appeal, totaling more than a thousand words. In short, it was believed that Zhou's killing of Li was premeditated, stating that Zhou Zhanyuan was usually fierce and addicted to gambling, disloyal to his duties, and committed more than four offenses, which led to Li's dismissal. Zhou handed over all the company's items to the head Zhu Delun, but did not hand over the pistol. He also wandered in the corridor for a long time before killing Li. Afterwards, he knew that the puppet state was a good place to avoid punishment. His intentional murder was self-evident. However, the first instance relied on Zhou's one-sided words and believed that it was not premeditated, which was very inappropriate. Therefore, the appeal was filed, requesting the abolition of the principle and a change of sentence to capital punishment, etc. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yu, accompanied by two judges Zhao and Zhou, opened a criminal court to interrogate him. Li Min and Zhou's family also hired lawyer Chen Tingrui to appear in court. After questioning by the court, the court ordered a change of date for further trial.

The First Step of the China-America Tobacco Company's Plan is Successful 158

The Second Step of the Plan Begins

Dinner for the Press of This City Last Night

At the beginning of the establishment of the China-America Tobacco Company, in view of the huge surplus of imported cigarettes, the company adhered to the purpose of promoting domestic products and worked hard to manage the company in order to recover rights. The initial plan was to create two famous brands of cigarettes within six months. So far, the two types of cigarettes, the Blue Major Commander and the Red Major Commander, which have been in operation for six months, have been welcomed for their good quality and low price, and they have indeed sold well in various places as scheduled. The first step of the plan has been successful. The second step of the plan will focus on the recently launched Ginseng brand and the soon-to-be-launched Guanghua brand. The company's general manager Jing Yimeng, associates Wang Yongchang, Yu Zhong'e, and others, in between the success of the first step of the plan and the start of the second step of the plan, yesterday evening specially invited the press of this city to Huaan to a dinner. Those who attended included Zhao Junhao, Ma Chonggan, Sun Enlin, Qian Hua, Jin Huating, Zhu Mingxin, Sun Daosheng from Shen Bao, Yu Kongwo, Jiang Jianhou, Jiang Zongyi, Fan Jingwu, Li Zutang from Xinwen Bao, Hu Hanzhu, Jiang Zongdao from Shibao, Huang Tianpeng, Yuan Xifan, Zhu Manhua from Shishi Xinbao, Xu Xingchu, Xu Zhuodai from Chen Bao, Guan Jiu'an, Wu Zhongyi, Jiang Hongjiao from Min Bao, Yao Tingchun from Da Wan Bao, and more than 30 other people. The company's staff warmly entertained them. During the banquet, General Manager Jing Yimeng reported on the company's organizational history (speech attached below). Next, Xu Zhuodai and Wu Zhongyi delivered thank-you speeches on behalf of the press. Finally, the company presented Red and Blue Major Commander Ginseng and other cigarettes. Jing Yimeng's speech is as follows: "It is an honor to have you here today. Our company was founded in the summer of last year and has only been in operation for more than half a year. It is still in its infancy. Today, we specially invite you to come and guide us, so that we can use it as a compass for future progress. Now, I will report to you the company's situation in the past six months. The establishment of our company was originally of a trial nature. It was initiated with accidental interest, and the initiators were mostly colleagues from Huaan Cooperative Life Insurance Company and Guanghua and Mei Da oil companies. Therefore, it was named Huamei. At that time, there were two trial purposes: First, because various industries are currently in a downturn, although cigarettes are consumer goods, their consumption is so large that it is one of the major industries. The people of our country consume about 200 million yuan on this every year, and 60% of them are produced by foreign tobacco companies, while Chinese merchants only account for 40%. Our colleagues believe that if we can do our best to recover rights and prevent leaks, we will gain an inch or a foot. However, at this time of market downturn, whether we can achieve one in ten thousand effects by fighting the environment, let's use this as a trial. Second, what kind of power is the promotion and development of cigarettes based on? If there is an existing brand, its brand name and the quality of the tobacco leaves are not inferior, but the reason why it cannot be sold well may be due to limited economic relations. Then, can we find a way to revitalize it and make the promotion effective? At that time, the Major Commander brand of cigarettes made by Shanghai Tobacco Company could not be fully developed due to the impact of the January 28th Incident. Therefore, the company transferred the production and sales rights of this brand to our company. Our company is also happy to accept it as a trial. Fortunately, in the past six months, this Major Commander cigarette has been approved by all sectors of society. Its sales volume has increased from 200 boxes per month to 700 boxes, and the quantity purchased by managers in various places has increased monthly, and there is a trend of development. Therefore, colleagues believe that the above two points of the trial are still effective. After this, we should work harder. However, outsiders do not know that because our company is named Huamei, it is suspected that there are foreign shareholders. I don't know that the name of our company is because it was initiated by colleagues from the above-mentioned three companies, so it has this name. The capital is entirely Chinese shares and has been registered with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce in accordance with the law. It can be seen that the rumors from the outside are all false. Also, although the brand name of Major Commander is translated from English, this brand was originally created by Shanghai Tobacco Company, and the company is also a Chinese merchant and a member of the Chinese Cigarette Guild. The brand is now produced and sold by our company, and of course it is still a domestic product. There are outsiders who mistakenly believe that it is a foreign brand, which is a misunderstanding. For the above points, I would like to ask you to explain in the newspapers to dispel public doubts. It would be greatly appreciated. Our company's trial has been slightly successful, so we have expanded our capital since this year and made new brands by ourselves. The Ginseng brand has now been launched, and the Guanghua brand will also be launched soon. I hope that in the era of promoting domestic products, we will do our best to promote the development of domestic products. However, our company's colleagues have very shallow talent and experience. I still ask the gentlemen of the public opinion circle to give us advice at any time. I am very grateful. I would like to propose a toast to wish you good health."

Two Examples of Encouraging the Song Dynasty Canon 162

Since the launch of the pre-order for the reproduction of the Song Dynasty Qisha Edition of the Great Canon, each copy is only priced at 525 yuan, which is less than one-tenth of the price of the Qing Dynasty Dragon Canon printed in Beiping. Therefore, famous temples, major libraries, and book collectors have paid to order from the Shanghai (714 Weihaiwei Road) Reproduction of the Song Edition Canon Association. Among them, there are two examples of pooling funds, which can be used as models for those who have faith and willingness but lack the financial resources to follow suit. They are recorded as follows: (A) Hongyi Chan Returns to the Record of Xiamen Poor Children Donating Funds to Request the Song Dynasty Canon: In June of the 22nd year of the summer calendar, the Miaoshi Temple in Xiamen raised funds to request the Song Dynasty Qisha Canon. After it was advocated, on the 15th, a poor mother brought her son to the monk's room and donated one yuan, saying that she wanted to help request the Song Dynasty Canon with this. When asked who gave it, she said the child gave it. When asked how the one yuan was obtained, she said the mother often gave the child one penny to ask for what he needed. The child did not waste it, but gathered and stored it. The mother gave it many times, and over the years, it became one penny, gradually filling one yuan. He had kept it in his arms for a long time, regarding it as a treasure. Today, he accompanied his mother to the temple to worship Buddha. When he heard others say that they were raising funds to request the Song Dynasty Canon, he was delighted and danced, praising it as a great opportunity. So he gave up what he treasured and rejoiced. The child was wearing torn clothes, barefoot without shoes, and had not yet reached childhood. His name was Wu Yi. Written by Shamen Hongyi Yinyin in the first month of Jiaxu. (B) The Guangxi Guiping Buddhist Research Society's Method of Encouraging the Request of the Song Dynasty Canon: (1) Initiated by the Guiping Buddhist Research Society, requesting the purchase of a Tibetan of the Shanghai reproduced Song Dynasty Qisha Sutras, totaling 6,310 volumes (1) The funds for requesting the sutras will be raised by the Buddhist Research Society issuing donation books to encourage subscriptions (1) The donation procedures are in accordance with the Forty-Eight Vows of Amitabha Buddha. Forty-eight donation books will be printed, one for each vow. Each book is limited to a donation of 25 cents (this is the Guangxi cent silver conversion, so this number is required). Those who receive the donation book must donate at least one yuan. The remaining 48 people will donate 50 cents each to complete one vow. However, for convenience, the person who receives the book can design and encourage donations at will, and must complete the vow (1) The donation receipt is first stamped by the Buddhist Research Society, and then signed and stamped by the handler (1) The deadline for returning the donation book is one month from the date of receipt, so that it can be remitted early and fulfill the pre-order (1) In addition to properly arranging the scriptures this time, the remaining funds will print the names of the kind men and women into a booklet according to the amount of donation, together with the scriptures, to be immortalized. Those who donate more than 5 yuan will be sent back a booklet, along with a scripture reading ticket, as a souvenir. Those who donate 50 cents up to 5 yuan will only be sent a scripture reading ticket and not a name list to save money. As for those who take on the responsibility of encouraging donations or donate one vow or more by themselves, in addition to sending booklets and tickets, the fundraising committee will present a silver-plated Amitabha Buddha commemorative badge, and those who recognize five to ten vows or more will be invited to take photos of the donors to hang on the Sutra Library to commemorate and promote virtue forever.

Thirty Cigarette Factories Send Letter to Association, Urging Swift Change to Cigarette Tax System 163

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, after twenty-four locally owned cigarette factories in this city jointly petitioned the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Finance, Tax Affairs Administration, to change the new cigarette tax system, the Tax Affairs Administration immediately sent a letter to the city's Cigarette Factory Trade Association for a reply. Now, the following thirty factories:

Minzhong Tobacco Company, Yuxin Tobacco Factory, Datongnan Tobacco Company, Huaqing Tobacco Company, Jinsha Tobacco Factory, Huadong Tobacco Company, Jiangzhejian Company, Guochang Tobacco Company, Kefu Tobacco Company, Ximen Tobacco Company, Fuxin Tobacco Company, Huaxing Tobacco Company, Huamei Tobacco Company, Asia Tobacco Company, Shanghai Tobacco Company, Dada Tobacco Factory, Delong Tobacco Company, Xinmin Tobacco Company, Huapin Tobacco Company, Daxing Tobacco Company, Youli Tobacco Company, Changming Tobacco Company, Fuchang Tobacco Company, Jinshan Tobacco Company, Huafu Tobacco Company, Yonghe Tobacco Company, Jiuyi Tobacco Factory, Jiangnan Tobacco Company, Meixing Tobacco Company, and Minsheng Tobacco Company, have jointly prepared a letter of opinion and submitted it to the Trade Association, requesting that it promptly reply to the Tax Affairs Administration to improve the tax rate as soon as possible. The full text of the letter of opinion is as follows: Regarding the proposal, after investigating the joint petition from twenty-four tobacco companies, including Minzhong, regarding the current unequal treatment of Chinese and foreign cigarette taxes, we request a swift revision of the tax grades to provide relief. The Ministry of Finance, Tax Affairs Administration, has now sent a letter to the Shanghai Chinese Factory Trade Association for a reply. This case is of great importance to the survival of the Chinese cigarette industry. Ziping and others have repeatedly studied it and believe that the statistical tables submitted by Minzhong and other companies are based on the statistical bulletin and tax bulletin compiled by the Tax Affairs Administration. Since these bulletins are issued by the Tax Affairs Administration, the numbers listed are certainly accurate. According to this statistic, changing from a three-tier tax to a two-tier tax not only creates unequal treatment for Chinese and foreign companies but also greatly reduces government tax revenue. In the era of the three-tier tax, British and American cigarette sales used 30,472 stamps. In the era of the two-tier tax, they used 48,808 stamps. According to the unified tax regulations, one stamp is used for each box of cigarettes. Therefore, in the era of the two-tier tax, the number of British and American cigarette taxes increased by 18,336 boxes compared to the era of the three-tier tax, an increase of more than 50%. If the government still collects taxes according to the three-tier tax rate, without any reduction, tax revenue will definitely increase by more than 50%. In the era of the three-tier tax, the average monthly tax payment for British and American companies was more than 2.41 million yuan. If we conservatively estimate an increase of 50%, the monthly increase should be more than 1.2 million yuan. Therefore, the monthly tax payment for British and American companies should be more than 3.61 million yuan. However, according to the facts, in the era of the two-tier tax, the average monthly tax payment for British and American companies is only more than 2.72 million yuan. Comparing the two, the government actually collects 890,000 yuan less each month. This is the result of the tax reduction on high-end cigarettes. From this perspective, with the three-tier tax changed to a two-tier tax, the government collects 890,000 yuan less per month from British and American companies, and 10.68 million yuan less per year. Can it be said that this is not a loss for the government? If we talk about Chinese companies, in the era of the three-tier tax, other tobacco companies used 68,422 cigarette stamps. In the era of the two-tier tax, they used 44,323 stamps. Therefore, in the era of the two-tier tax, the number of cigarette sales of other tobacco companies decreased by about one-third. If the government still collects taxes according to the three-tier tax rate, without any reduction, tax revenue will naturally decrease by one-third. In the era of the three-tier tax, the average monthly tax payment for other tobacco companies was more than 2 million yuan. If it decreases by one-third, it should decrease by more than 660,000 yuan, which should be more than 1.34 million yuan. However, according to the facts, in the era of the two-tier tax, the average monthly tax payment for other tobacco companies is actually more than 2.55 million yuan. Comparing the two, Chinese companies increase their burden by 1.21 million yuan per month, and a total increase of 14.52 million yuan per year. This is the result of the tax increase on low-end cigarettes. Based on this comprehensive calculation, after the implementation of the two-tier tax, British and American cigarette sales have increased by an average of two-fifths, but the tax revenue has decreased by 10.68 million yuan throughout the year. Chinese cigarette sales have decreased by an average of one-third, but the tax revenue has increased by 14.52 million yuan throughout the year. Can it be said that this is not unequal treatment for Chinese and foreign companies? At this time of suppressing bandits and building the nation,

Chinese Merchants, for the Party and the Nation, Increase the Burden, We Dare Not Refuse. However, based on the above figures, the government collects 14.52 million yuan more from Chinese companies throughout the year, but collects 10.68 million yuan less from British and American companies. Therefore, by changing from a three-tier tax to a two-tier tax, the government's income is only 3.84 million yuan throughout the year, while British and American companies' income is actually 10.68 million yuan, almost three times the government's income. As a result of the two-tier tax, in terms of the entire cigarette tax, Chinese companies are the victims, British and American companies account for 75% of the beneficiaries, and the government only accounts for 25%. In terms of the government's tax revenue from British and American companies, the government is the complete victim, while British and American companies are the beneficiaries. Alas, Chinese companies are exhausted and bear more than 14.5 million yuan in heavy taxes throughout the year. If every drop belongs to the government, what can we say? Now, British and American companies are allowed to enjoy a profit of 10.68 million yuan every year, which is tantamount to extracting the blood and sweat of Chinese companies to supply British and American companies. British and American companies take advantage of this opportunity to extract the income of Chinese companies and drastically reduce prices to encroach on the market. Therefore, in one year, the quantity of cigarettes produced by British and American companies has suddenly increased by 50%, while Chinese companies have closed down one after another, from 150-160 companies to 40-50 companies. Although the loss of Chinese companies' taxes is only more than 14.5 million yuan, the loss of business is unknown by how many millions of yuan. Although the benefit of British and American companies' taxes is only more than 10 million yuan, the profit of business is again unknown by how many millions. However, this is still only in terms of the cigarette industry. If we talk about domestic tobacco leaves, the loss is also not small. Low-end cigarettes are all made of domestic leaves. Low-end cigarettes are not competitive due to heavy taxes, and domestic tobacco leaves will inevitably be unsalable. According to the statistics of Minzhong and other tobacco companies, the domestic tobacco leaves produced in Susong, Huanggang, Xinchang, Dengzhou, Guanshui, and Junzhou amounted to about 390,000 packages per year during the seven-tier tax era before 1930. After the three-tier tax was changed in November 1930, it decreased to 260,000 packages. After the two-tier tax was changed in 1932, it decreased again to 115,000 packages. Recently, after the tax was changed, it was heard that this tobacco leaf

Is Almost Unattended. Jiujiang and Laohekou Tax Affairs Administrations have established offices for domestic tobacco. We plan to forward a letter to the Tax Affairs Administration, ordering them to investigate and respond, and we will be able to obtain the truth. Under the current tax system, domestic tobacco is taxed at 4.14 yuan per 100 jin. If it is not sold because of this, what is the loss of government tax revenue? How much does the rural economy lose when tobacco farmers go bankrupt as a result? This is also not something that can be calculated with numbers. I believe that the mistake of the two-tier tax is entirely due to the tax reduction on high-end cigarettes and the tax increase on low-end cigarettes. High-end cigarettes are expensive, and low-end cigarettes are cheap. In terms of the seven-tier tax, the selling price of each box of high-end cigarettes is 1052 yuan, and the tax is 404 yuan. The selling price of each box of seven-tier cigarettes is 125 yuan, and the tax is 29 yuan. This is based on the principle of equal taxation, taxing according to value. The tax on one box of high-end cigarettes is enough to offset more than a dozen boxes of low-end cigarettes. Therefore, in order to have sufficient tax revenue, even if we do not focus on high-end cigarettes, we must treat high, medium, and low-end cigarettes equally. We must never focus solely on low-end cigarettes. Now, let us assume that the government must raise 3.8 million yuan in cigarette tax. If it does not solely blame the low-end cigarettes of Chinese merchants and also lets the high-end cigarettes of British and American companies share the burden, then let us take a step back and calculate at half of each. Chinese merchants only need to increase their burden by 1.9 million yuan. Why should they bear the heavy tax of more than 14 million yuan? If we say that regardless of the people's ability to pay, Chinese merchants must bear more than 14 million yuan in taxes, and British and American companies must also bear the same amount, then British and American cigarette sales are more than those of Chinese merchants, and what they sell are expensive high-end cigarettes. If we increase the tax according to value, the tax payment of British and American companies will simultaneously increase by more than 30 million yuan. The government's income can then increase by 50 million yuan annually. Therefore, for the sake of increasing tax revenue, the government must levy the same tax on high, medium, and low-end cigarettes. The principle is very simple. As for the two-tier tax, the tax increase on low-end cigarettes is too heavy, and the tax rate on high-end cigarettes is too light, only causing endless losses to Chinese merchants,

While British and American Companies Enjoy Huge Profits. It can truly be said to have hundreds of harms and not a single benefit. However, this is still in terms of the two-tier tax of 1932. If we consider the current two-tier tax, first-tier cigarettes are extremely rare, almost zero. What is actually collected is only the second tier, which is equivalent to only one tax grade. The price of low-end cigarettes has increased from 55 yuan per box to 80 yuan per box, which is even more than before. The price of high-end cigarettes has decreased from 95 yuan per box to 80 yuan per box, which is less than before. It has not been implemented for long now. What are the losses of Chinese merchants? What are the benefits of British and American companies? We have not obtained clear statistical figures. However, based on previous methods, the loss of Chinese merchants should be more than 20 million yuan per year, and the benefit of British and American companies should be at least 16-17 million yuan. If we must continue to implement it, we will see that these remaining 40-50 Chinese companies will also close down one after another, and all domestic tobacco leaves will be eliminated. Tobacco farmers in Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui will then go bankrupt. Therefore, it is urgent to catch up and abolish it immediately, without allowing any hesitation. Some say that, as mentioned above, under the current tax system, low-end cigarettes are taxed at 80 yuan per box, and high and medium-end cigarettes are appropriately increased according to grade. Isn't this a clever trick to raise funds? Then, I think not. The tax of 80 yuan per box on low-end cigarettes is a heavy tax of 120% of the value, which the people cannot afford at this time. In recent years, Chinese merchants have closed down one after another, which is the result of low-end cigarettes being unable to bear the heavy tax. If we impose a heavy tax of 120% of the value on high and medium-end cigarettes, we are ordering the entire tobacco industry to perish together. The government and tobacco merchants will both suffer. There is no feasible reason. The only plan is to adopt the principle of equal burden for high, medium, and low-end cigarettes, and the tax rate should be handled moderately. The newly set two-tier tax rate, with high-end cigarettes at 36% of the value and low-end cigarettes at 120% of the value, is both too light and too heavy. If we appropriately change it to a uniform 50-60% of the value, the burden on tobacco merchants will be relatively fair. The government's tax revenue will decrease on low-end cigarettes, but it will greatly increase on high and medium-end cigarettes, which will benefit the national treasury. The public association does not have accurate records of the selling price and sales volume of various cigarette brands. The government has not announced them either. Ziping and others

Have No Way to Calculate Based On. The Tax Affairs Administration should have accurate registration. If we negotiate based on this principle, we will be able to set a fair and appropriate tax rate. As for what the Tax Affairs Administration's letter emphasizes, there are a total of three points: (1) Whether the tax revenue is affected; (2) Whether the opinions of the industry are consistent; (3) Whether there are obstacles to the implementation in practice. Ziping and others have repeatedly discussed this and respectfully answered as follows: (1) Whether the tax revenue is affected. As mentioned earlier, the failure of the two-tier tax lies in the tax reduction on high-end cigarettes. Therefore, the income from the tax increase on low-end cigarettes must still make up for the loss of the tax reduction on high-end cigarettes. Although the burden on Chinese merchants is heavy, the government does not benefit from it, because British and American companies enjoy the benefit of a tax reduction of more than 10 million yuan every year. If we break the idea of benefiting from the tax reduction on high-end cigarettes and appropriately increase the tax rate on high and medium-end cigarettes, then the benefit of the tax reduction that British and American companies have enjoyed every year must be returned to the government. We will see the daily increase in tax revenue. How can there be any talk of affecting tax revenue? (2) Whether the opinions of the industry are consistent. People's hearts are different, and each has its own face. It is impossible for the opinions of the industry to be consistent in fact. Let's try to make an analogy. Most Chinese people do not approve of the establishment of Manchukuo, but Zheng Xiaoxu and Shi Yousan, who were attached to the puppet regime, are also Chinese people. It is impossible for the world to say that Zheng Shi's attachment to the puppet regime means that the Chinese people are not consistent and should recognize Manchukuo. Therefore, when discussing the cigarette tax rate, we should only ask whether it is in line with the principle of fairness and whether it is harmless to our country's agriculture, industry, and commerce. We do not need to ask whether the industry is consistent. If a tax rate is in line with the principle of fairness and does not harm our country's industry, it should be adopted. Otherwise, it should be abolished. Whether the industry is consistent is not important. If it is said that it must be consistent, then under the current two-tier tax, twenty-four cigarette companies in Shanghai, including Minzhong, do not agree with it. Cigarette companies in Hebei, Shandong, Shanxi, Henan, and other provinces have also opposed it one after another. It should have been abolished long ago. Therefore, this section does not need to be discussed. (3) Whether there are obstacles to the implementation in practice. This is probably due to concerns about the opposition of British and American companies. It is actually not worth worrying about. Before the establishment of the National Government, tariffs were restricted to 5% of the value. After the tariff autonomy, this unequal treaty has been broken. The consolidated tax is an internal tax. In the era of diplomatic failure of the Qing Dynasty, internal taxes were never interfered with by foreigners. China is originally an autonomous country. No matter how strong foreign merchants are, they can never interfere with internal taxes. Even based on the agreement between the Tax Affairs Administration and British and American companies, it only states that they must receive the same treatment as Chinese factories. There is no special preferential clause. If we set a fair tax rate that is consistent for Chinese and foreign companies and taxes according to value, we do not need to worry about foreigners making excuses. The above is what Ziping and others have thoroughly studied and agreed on. Now that the Tax Affairs Administration is soliciting the opinions of tobacco merchants and the members' meeting is studying the tax rate, it is reasonable to prepare a letter of opinion and submit it to the meeting, hoping that you will carefully review it, reply to the Tax Affairs Administration, and strive to improve the tax rate as soon as possible to save Chinese merchants from hanging upside down. The industry will be very grateful. This is addressed to the Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Factory Trade Association Members' Meeting.

Huge Advance Payment Leads to Financial Circulation Problems

Another Letter to the Tax Affairs Administration, Requesting Accommodation and Approval

Since the Ministry of Finance increased the consolidated tax on matches, the National Match Industry Trade Association, due to its difficult situation and inability to comply with the order, has again sent a letter to the Ministry of Finance and the Tax Affairs Administration. The original text is recorded as follows: We respectfully reply that we recently received Letter No. 2576 from your department, which roughly stated that regarding our association's previous letter requesting that the date for recording tax payments be appropriately extended, the tax payment recording was originally scheduled for the 25th of each month, which is already an extraordinary accommodation. At this time of extreme treasury shortage, even in terms of military supplies, it is difficult to cope with adequately. If the tax payments due from each of the tax-paying manufacturers can be recorded for as long as three months, once this precedent is set, how can we take care of the national treasury expenditure? The request is not approved, etc. Upon receiving this, the case was not approved, and we should obey. However, the match industry has been declining in recent years due to the dumping of foreign-made matches and the unlimited establishment of factories. The current increase in the consolidated tax on matches is almost one and a half times the old tax. The burden on match manufacturers has suddenly increased. Match factories with smaller capital are facing even greater operating difficulties due to financial circulation problems. This is truly insufficient to provide relief. Our association is not unaware of the current treasury shortage and the huge amount of military supplies. Therefore, after the tax increase was implemented, although we knew that it would be difficult for all members to shoulder this burden, we did not rashly request to withdraw the decision. However, recently, all members have been stretched thin and unable to maintain operations. We had no choice but to request an extension of the tax payment recording date. Our association and all members believe that this method can slightly help in terms of manufacturers' capital operation without affecting government tax revenue. It is truly a comprehensive and prudent method. However, we have still failed to receive accommodation and approval. If all members are exhausted and forced to close down one after another in the future, then hundreds of thousands of match workers will suddenly become unemployed, which is not a blessing for the country or society. At the same time, the collection of consolidated tax on matches will also be affected, which is far from the original intention of your department to increase taxes. Our association is a united group of match industries across the country. We have a better understanding of the advantages and disadvantages of this matter. We dare not use alarming words to scare people. The above is all factual information. We especially do not avoid bothering you and submit another letter, earnestly requesting your department to carefully observe the facts, carefully consider the advantages and disadvantages, and still approve the tax payment recording date to be appropriately extended. If this method is truly difficult to accommodate and approve, please also devise other relief methods to open a line of survival for match manufacturers, so that more than a hundred match factories will not close down and hundreds of thousands of match workers will not become unemployed. The country will be fortunate, and the match industry will be fortunate. We are extremely eager to await your orders. This is addressed to the Ministry of Finance Tax Affairs Administration, respectfully submitted by the National Match Industry United Association of China.
